# math.NA [[Back]](#toc)

### [1] [Finite element exponential integration for rough solutions of nonlinear wave equations. Part II: Dynamic boundary conditions on curved domains](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18320)
*Jiachuan Cao,Benjamin Dörich,Buyang Li*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 本文针对光滑有界域上具有动态边界条件的非线性波动方程，提出并分析了低正则性框架下的全离散逼近方法。该方法结合k次等参体-表面有限元与指数时间积分器，在仅假设精确解能量有界的条件下，证明了位移-速度对在弱范数L²(Ω;Γ)×H⁻¹(Ω;Γ)下的收敛性，实现了时间一阶收敛和空间h^{2/3}(k=1)及h^{(k+2)/(k+3)}(k≥2)阶收敛。通过发展基于提升和伴随提升算子的弱范数框架处理非协调几何，这是首个针对非协调体-表面有限元设置的非线性波动方程动态边界条件的全离散低正则性收敛结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有数值方法处理具有动态边界条件的非线性波动方程时，通常需要较高的正则性假设，且体-表面有限元方法面临连续与离散问题定义在不同几何上的非协调性挑战。本文旨在低正则性条件下建立严格的全离散收敛理论，并证明高阶有限元即使在低正则性下仍具有渐进优势。

Method: 采用k次等参体-表面有限元进行空间离散，结合指数时间积分器进行全离散化。针对几何非协调性，发展基于提升(ift)和伴随提升(adjoint-lift)算子的弱范数分析框架，结合频率分解论证，在仅假设能量有界的条件下实现弱范数收敛性分析。

Result: 证明了位移-速度对在L²(Ω;Γ)×H⁻¹(Ω;Γ)弱范数下的收敛性：时间一阶收敛，空间收敛阶为h^{2/3}(k=1)和h^{(k+2)/(k+3)}(k≥2)。数值实验验证了理论预测的收敛率，并展示了高阶方法的效率优势。

Conclusion: 本文首次在非协调体-表面有限元框架下建立了非线性波动方程动态边界条件的全离散低正则性收敛结果，证明了高阶有限元在低正则性下仍具有理论上的渐进优势，为相关问题的数值分析提供了新工具。

Abstract: We study nonlinear wave equations with dynamic boundary conditions on smooth bounded domains and analyze a fully discrete approximation in the low-regularity regime. The method combines isoparametric bulk--surface finite elements of degree $k$ with an exponential integrator in time. Assuming only bounded energy of the exact solution, we prove convergence of the displacement--velocity pair in the weak norm $L^2(Ω;Γ)\times H^{-1}(Ω;Γ)$. The scheme achieves first-order convergence in time and spatial convergence of order $h^{2/3}$ for $k=1$ and $h^{(k+2)/(k+3)}$ for $k\ge 2$. In particular, these rates show that higher-order finite elements retain a provable asymptotic advantage even at low regularity. A central difficulty is that the continuous and discrete bulk--surface problems are posed on different geometries and must therefore be compared directly in weak norms. To address this, we develop a weak-norm framework for non-conforming geometries based on lift and adjoint-lift operators, combined with a frequency-decomposition argument. To the best of our knowledge, this is the first fully discrete low-regularity convergence result for nonlinear wave equations with dynamic boundary conditions in a non-conforming bulk--surface finite element setting. Numerical experiments confirm the predicted rates and illustrate the improved efficiency of higher-order methods.

</details>


### [2] [Convergence and almost sure exponential stability of compensated split-step theta scheme for stochastic pantograph models with Poisson random measure](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18327)
*Amr Abosenna,Yongchun Zhou,Boping Tian*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 本文针对带有泊松随机测度的随机比例模型，采用补偿分裂步theta方法进行数值求解，证明了数值格式的非发散性、收敛性以及几乎必然指数稳定性，并通过数值算例验证了理论结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随机比例模型在金融、生物、控制和随机神经网络等领域有广泛应用，且随机微分方程中引入跳过程更符合实际需求，因此需要对该类模型进行数值分析和稳定性研究。

Method: 采用补偿分裂步theta（compensated split-step theta）数值格式对带有泊松随机测度的随机比例模型进行离散化处理。

Result: 在给定假设条件下，数值格式具有非发散性，并收敛到原模型解；利用离散半鞅收敛定理证明了数值解的几乎必然指数稳定性。

Conclusion: 补偿分裂步theta方法是求解带有泊松跳的随机比例模型的有效数值方案，具有良好的稳定性和收敛性，数值实验支持理论分析结果。

Abstract: Recently, stochastic pantograph models have gained an intensive attention and have been used in different fields such as finance, biology, control and stochastic neural networks. It is also more preferable to incorporate jumps during the study of stochastic differential equations. In this paper, stochastic pantograph model with Poisson random measure is studied. The compensated split-step theta technique is applied to the considered model. The numerical scheme exhibits a non divergent attitude and converges to the solution of our model under assumptions addressed later on. Furthermore, the almost sure exponential stability of the numerical scheme is investigated via utilizing the discrete semi-martingale convergence theorem. Finally, theoretical findings are manifested via some numerical examples.

</details>


### [3] [A Second-Moment Theory for Floating-Point Reduction Trees](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18758)
*Piyush Sao,Narasinga Miniskar,Pedro Valero-Lara,Keita Teranishi,Sudip Seal*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 本文推导了二元归约树在条件无偏舍入下的精确均方误差递推关系，定义了共同祖先核矩阵K_T，并利用树结构统计量Λ₁和Λ₂刻画了误差与树拓扑的关系。文章给出了最优树结构、最优调度策略，并将该框架推广到矩阵乘法。实验验证了模型在多种浮点精度下对误差排序的预测能力，但指出了正数低精度求和中的停滞与偏差问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准舍入误差最坏情况上界忽略了求和顺序对误差的影响，现有分析无法捕捉树拓扑结构带来的误差差异。本文旨在建立一个能够精确刻画归约树结构对均方舍入误差影响的解析框架。

Method: 在条件无偏舍入假设下，推导二元归约树T的均方误差递推关系；引入常数-nu模型设定局部方差；定义共同祖先核K_T，将误差表达为p^T K_T p；对i.i.d.输入分解为τ²Λ₁(T)+μ²Λ₂(T)；通过变分法求解最优树结构；扩展至矩阵乘法中的Gram矩阵；在多种浮点精度下进行实验验证。

Result: 平衡树和顺序树分别达到中心化输入下误差的极小和极大；两阶段顺序封锁的RMS误差标度为k^{3/4}；对于固定阶段分层结构，几何调度对中心化输入最优，非中心化输入的最优阶段指数逐次减半；Huffman编码最小化方差加权深度；模型在binary64/32/16和bfloat16下正确复现树拓扑间的误差排序；GEMM预测与实测偏差不超过3%。

Conclusion: 本文建立了一个能够精确刻画归约树拓扑结构对舍入均方误差影响的解析框架，给出了多种场景下的最优树结构和调度策略。模型在实际浮点精度下具有良好的预测能力，但正数低精度求和中存在的停滞与偏差问题限制了其适用性。

Abstract: Summation error depends on partial-sum order, which standard worst-case bounds omit. To capture this dependence, we derive an exact mean-square error (MSE) recurrence for a binary reduction tree T under conditionally unbiased rounding. With unit roundoff u, the constant-nu model sets the local variance at pre-rounding value x to nu u^2 x^2. Its leading tree-dependent cost for the input vector p is p^T K_T p, where the common-ancestor kernel K_T counts the internal ancestors shared by each pair of leaves. For i.i.d. inputs of mean mu and variance tau^2, this expected cost is tau^2 Lambda_1(T) + mu^2 Lambda_2(T), where Lambda_1 is total leaf depth and Lambda_2 sums squared internal-subtree sizes; Lambda_1 governs centered inputs, while Lambda_2 captures nonzero means. We use these statistics to characterize optimal tree topologies and schedules. Balanced and sequential trees attain the centered extrema. For k inputs, optimal two-stage sequential blocking yields root-mean-square (RMS) error scaling as k^{3/4}. For fixed-stage hierarchies, geometric schedules are optimal for centered inputs, whereas the optimal noncentered stage exponents halve successively. For independent centered inputs with unequal variances, Huffman coding minimizes variance-weighted depth over free leaf assignments. We extend the kernel to matrix multiplication through operand Gram matrices. We then test the approximation under round-to-nearest using exact residuals. Across binary64, binary32, and software-emulated binary16 and bfloat16, the model recovers the ordering among tree topologies; K_T tracks AR(1) partial-sum costs. For GEMM, independently calibrated predictions differ from measurements by at most 3% on the tested grid. A reduction tree extracted from an array library predicts the measured RMS scaling. However, stagnation and bias in positive low-precision sums limit the model's applicability.

</details>


### [4] [Error Bound and Stability Analysis for a Randomized Singly Diagonally Implicit Runge-Kutta Method](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18928)
*Monika Eisenmann,Marvin Jans,Raphael Kruse,Helmut Podhaisky*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 提出了一种基于随机化梯形规则的随机SDIRK方法，证明其在低正则性假设下均方根收敛阶为2.5，数值实验表明该方法对非光滑问题具有鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 针对非光滑问题中传统确定性数值方法收敛性受限的挑战，探索利用随机化技术提升低正则性条件下的收敛阶和鲁棒性。

Method: 基于随机化梯形规则构造随机SDIRK方法，每次实现均为代数稳定的至少二阶SDIRK方法，通过随机化引入额外正则性以获得更高收敛阶。

Result: 证明随机化方案在均方根意义下收敛阶为2.5（高于确定性方法的二阶），数值实验验证了对非光滑问题的鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 随机化SDIRK方法在低正则性条件下实现了超越传统确定性方法的收敛阶，为非光滑问题提供了新的高效数值求解工具。

Abstract: A randomized Singly Diagonally Implicit Runge-Kutta (SDIRK) method, based on the randomized trapezoidal rule as the underlying quadrature scheme, is proposed. Every realization of the scheme is an algebraically stable SDIRK method of at least second order. The main result is the proof that the randomized scheme converges with order 2.5 in the root mean square sense under low regularity assumptions. Numerical experiments illustrate the robustness of the new scheme when applied to nonsmooth problems.

</details>


### [5] [Space-time tensor-product finite element methods for parabolic problems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19107)
*Richard Löscher,Michael Reichelt,Olaf Steinbach*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 本文研究抛物型演化问题的时空Galerkin-Petrov格式与经典隐式时间步进方案的关系，揭示了时步方法在时空框架下可能出现的条件稳定性问题，并针对Aziz-Monk连续Galerkin方法（最低阶对应Crank-Nicolson格式）提供了详细的时空误差分析，特别分析了非光滑初值导致的性能退化，并通过时间分部积分导出了自然包含初值条件的伴随时空格式，在最低阶情况下实现了Rannacher型初值光滑化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典隐式时步方案在时步意义下稳定，但将其解释为时空算子方程时可能出现条件稳定性（常数依赖于时空网格尺寸比），且非光滑初值下时步方法的性能退化需要从时空框架进行系统分析。

Method: 采用时空Galerkin-Petrov变分框架，对Aziz-Monk连续Galerkin方法进行时空误差分析（涵盖高正则性和低正则性解），通过时间分部积分推导伴随时空格式，实现初值条件的自然变分嵌入，最低阶情形得到Rannacher型光滑化。

Result: 揭示了时步方法在时空框架下的条件稳定性机制；建立了高/低正则性解的统一时空误差估计；导出的伴随格式在最低阶自动实现初值光滑化，改善了非光滑初值的数值行为；数值实验验证了理论分析。

Conclusion: 时空变分框架为理解和改进传统时步方法（尤其是非光滑初值情形）提供了统一的理论工具，伴随格式的Rannacher光滑化策略可有效缓解条件稳定性问题。

Abstract: We study space-time Galerkin--Petrov formulations for parabolic evolution problems and their relation to classical implicit time-stepping schemes. Although such schemes are stable in the usual time-stepping sense, their interpretation as space-time operator equations may lead to conditional stability, with constants depending on the relation between temporal and spatial mesh sizes. We revisit this phenomenon for the continuous Galerkin method of Aziz and Monk, which yields the Crank--Nicolson scheme in the lowest-order case, and provide a detailed space-time error analysis for solutions of both high and low regularity. In particular, the space-time framework allows us to analyze the deteriorated behaviour of classical time-stepping methods for nonsmooth initial data. By applying integration by parts in time, we derive an adjoint space-time formulation that incorporates the initial condition in a natural variational way. In the lowest-order case, this formulation leads to a Rannacher-type smoothing of the initial data. The theoretical results are complemented by numerical experiments.

</details>


### [6] [Boundary-Adapted PINNs for Elliptic Dirichlet Problems: $H^2(Ω)$ A Priori Error Bounds with Application to Mean Escape Time Computation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19167)
*Nathanael Tepakbong,Jun Fan,Xiang Zhou,Ding-Xuan Zhou*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 本文针对有界域上的椭圆Dirichlet边值问题，研究了边界强制物理信息神经网络（PINNs）的误差分析。理论证明：仅靠精确边界强制不足以获得H²(Ω)误差界，需要距离函数ρ满足一阶归一化光滑近似条件。数值实验验证了恰当选择ρ能提高精度和收敛性，同时导出了ReQU和tanh网络的新VC维界和逼近界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 受随机过程平均逃逸时间（MET）数值计算驱动，研究如何通过边界强制的PINNs高效求解椭圆Dirichlet边值问题，并明确距离函数ρ对误差的影响机制。

Method: 结合逼近论和统计学习理论，对ReQU和tanh网络进行先验误差分析；通过将网络输出乘以预定义的边界距离近似ρ来精确强制Dirichlet边界条件；研究ρ的平滑性和归一化条件对H²(Ω)误差界的影响。

Result: 证明精确边界强制不足以保证H²(Ω)误差界，充要条件是ρ为一阶归一化的光滑距离近似；给出ReQU和tanh网络高阶导数假设空间的新VC维界，以及浅层ReQU网络高阶Sobolev范数的新逼近界。

Conclusion: 识别出"边界自适应"PINNs是求解Dirichlet边值问题的恰当神经网络ansatz类；恰当的ρ选择能显著提升精度，反之劣化；所导出的VC维界和逼近界具有独立的理论价值。

Abstract: Motivated by the numerical computation of the Mean Escape Time (MET) $τ:Ω\to\mathbb{R}$ of a stochastic process from a bounded domain $Ω\subseteq\mathbb{R}^d$, we study elliptic Dirichlet boundary value problems (BVPs) using boundary-enforced Physics-Informed Neural Networks (PINNs), in which the Dirichlet condition is imposed exactly by multiplying the network output with a predefined distance-to-boundary approximation $ρ$. Combining approximation-theoretic and statistical-learning arguments for Rectified Quadratic Unit (ReQU) and hyperbolic tangent (tanh) networks, we derive a priori error bounds that make explicit the dependence on $ρ$. In particular, we show that exact boundary enforcement alone is not enough for $H^2(Ω)$ error bounds, and that a sufficient and essentially necessary condition is for $ρ$ to be a smooth distance approximation $\textit{normalized to first order}$, of the kind constructed in arXiv:2104.08426 [math.NA]. We thereby identify this subclass of $\textit{boundary-adapted}$ PINNs as the appropriate neural network ansatz for solving Dirichlet BVPs. Numerical experiments support the theory, showing that appropriate choices of $ρ$ improve accuracy and convergence, while poorly chosen distance functions can substantially degrade the solution. Our proof also yields new VC-dimension bounds for hypothesis spaces of higher-order derivatives of ReQU and tanh networks, together with new approximation bounds for shallow ReQU networks in higher-order Sobolev norms, all of which are of important independent interest.

</details>


### [7] [Numerical methods for Langevin-type SPDE: an implicit Milstein approach and multilevel Monte Carlo techniques](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19188)
*Sascha Portaro,Carlos Vázquez*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 本文针对二维退化Langevin型随机偏微分方程，提出了一种半隐式Milstein有限差分格式，并结合多层蒙特卡洛方法，将计算复杂度从O(ε⁻⁵)降低至O(ε⁻³)。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二维退化Langevin型SPDEs在随机动力学和数学金融等领域有广泛应用，但因其混合确定-随机结构以及微分算子的退化性，数值求解存在挑战，需要发展高效稳定的数值方法。

Method: 提出半隐式Milstein有限差分格式；通过Fourier分析研究均方稳定性与收敛性，推导显式稳定条件与收敛速率；将所提格式嵌入多层蒙特卡洛框架以降低计算成本。

Result: 数值实验验证了理论收敛速率；MLMC策略在达到相同精度的前提下，将计算复杂度从标准MC的O(ε⁻⁵)降至O(ε⁻³)。

Conclusion: 半隐式Milstein格式与MLMC技术的结合为Langevin型SPDEs的数值模拟提供了一种有效途径，在保持精度的同时大幅提升计算效率。

Abstract: In this work, we investigate the numerical approximation of degenerate Langevin-type stochastic partial differential equations (SPDEs) in two spatial dimensions. These SPDEs arise in stochastic dynamics and mathematical finance, among other applications. In order to handle the mixed deterministic-stochastic structure of the equation and the degeneracy of the differential operator, we propose a semi-implicit Milstein finite difference scheme for the numerical solution.
  Through the Fourier analysis of the mean-square stability and convergence, we derive explicit conditions on the coefficients under which the scheme is stable, jointly with explicit convergence rates in terms of the discretization parameters. We further embed the proposed scheme within a Multilevel Monte Carlo (MLMC) framework to reduce the computational cost associated with SPDE simulations, and we derive its theoretical computational complexity.
  Numerical experiments confirm theoretical convergence rates and show that the MLMC strategy achieves an accuracy comparable to standard Monte Carlo at a fraction of the computational cost, reducing the complexity from $\mathcal{O}(\varepsilon^{-5})$ to $\mathcal{O}(\varepsilon^{-3})$ for a target root-mean-square error $\varepsilon$. These results show that combining semi-implicit Milstein schemes with MLMC techniques provides an effective approach for the numerical simulation of Langevin-type SPDEs.

</details>


### [8] [Uniform-in-Time Weak and Ergodic Error Estimates of a Nonlinearity-Explicit Full Discretization for Superlinear SPDEs Driven by Multiplicative Noise](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19250)
*Jingjing Cai,Zhihui Liu,Xiaoming Wu*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 本文针对乘性噪声驱动的超线性随机偏微分方程(SPDEs)，证明了非线性显式Galerkin驯服Euler方法(GTEM)的(本质上)尖锐的一致时间弱收敛速率。在标准单调性假设下，通过结合Malliavin微积分与向后Kolmogorov方程(BKE)的正则性理论，推导出UIT矩估计、Hölder估计、Malliavin估计以及BKE解的正则性估计，最终得到对任意ρ∈(0,1)的弱收敛速率τ^ρ+λ_N^{-ρ}，并获得了精确与数值不变测度之间的尖锐遍历误差估计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决超线性SPDEs数值方法在长时间模拟中的弱收敛速率问题，特别是获得一致时间(Uniform-in-Time)的收敛估计，以保障数值方法在遍历采样等长时间计算中的可靠性。

Method: 1) 采用非线性显式Galerkin驯服Euler方法(GTEM)进行数值离散；2) 结合Malliavin微积分与向后Kolmogorov方程的正则性理论；3) 建立UIT矩、Hölder和Malliavin估计；4) 通过弱误差分解与Malliavin分部积分公式导出弱收敛速率。

Result: 获得对任意ρ∈(0,1)的UIT弱收敛速率τ^ρ+λ_N^{-ρ}（τ为时间步长，λ_N为谱截断参数），并得到精确与数值不变测度之间的尖锐遍历误差估计。

Conclusion: 所提出的GTEM方法在超线性SPDEs上取得了本质上尖锐的一致时间弱收敛速率，为长时间数值模拟和不变测度的逼近提供了理论保证，数值实验验证了理论结果。

Abstract: For a class of superlinear SPDEs driven by multiplicative noise, we prove an (essentially) sharp uniform-in-time (UIT) weak convergence rate for the nonlinearity-explicit Galerkin tamed Euler method (GTEM). Under standard monotonicity assumptions, the proof combines Malliavin calculus with regularity theory for the associated backward Kolmogorov equation (BKE), leading to UIT moment, Hölder, and Malliavin estimates, along with regularity estimates for the BKE solution. These estimates, together with a weak error decomposition and Malliavin integration by parts (IBP) formula, then yield a UIT weak convergence rate $τ^ρ+λ_N^{-ρ}$ for any $ρ\in (0,1)$. Consequently, we obtain a sharp ergodic error estimate between the exact and numerical invariant measures. Numerical experiments support the theory.

</details>


### [9] [Weighted Inverse Lax-Wendroff Boundary Treatment of Discontinuous Galerkin Methods for Conservation Laws](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19258)
*Yongjie Bi,Yan Jiang,Yong Liu*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种加权逆Lax-Wendroff（WILW）边界处理方法，用于非拟合网格上的间断伽辽金（DG）方法，以高效求解复杂几何区域中的双曲守恒律。该方法通过提高边界重构阶数消除数值误差对切割单元几何尺寸的敏感性，并采用加权最小二乘重构减少高阶边界导数的计算需求，从而在保持高阶精度的同时显著提升计算效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决非拟合网格上DG方法处理双曲守恒律时，小切割单元导致的严格时间步长限制以及基本ILW方案中数值误差对切割单元几何尺寸敏感的问题，同时降低高阶边界导数构造的复杂性。

Method: 采用标准DG格式处理内部单元，对边界附近的切割单元基于ILW原理重构高阶逼近多项式以施加数值边界条件；通过提高边界重构阶数使精度独立于切割单元尺寸；引入加权最小二乘重构以减少构造过程中对复杂高阶边界导数的需求。

Result: 通过线性稳定性分析验证了方法的理论稳定性；通过一系列一维和二维标量方程及方程组数值实验，验证了该方法在高阶精度保持、计算效率提升以及鲁棒性方面的有效性。

Conclusion: WILW边界处理方法有效消除了小切割单元导致的时间步长限制和误差敏感性，在保持高阶精度的同时显著提升了多维问题的计算效率，为复杂几何区域中的双曲守恒律数值求解提供了一种稳健高效的方案。

Abstract: In this paper, we propose a weighted inverse Lax-Wendroff (WILW) boundary treatment for the discontinuous Galerkin (DG) method on unfitted meshes to efficiently solve hyperbolic conservation laws in complex geometries. The proposed method employs the standard DG scheme for interior cells and reconstructs high-order approximation polynomials via the ILW principle for cut cells near boundaries to impose numerical boundary conditions, effectively eliminating the time-step restriction typically caused by small cut cells. In particular, to address the sensitivity of numerical errors to the geometric size of cut cells in the basic ILW scheme, we raise the reconstruction order at the boundary, ensuring that accuracy becomes independent of the cut-cell size. Furthermore, it incorporates a weighted least-squares reconstruction to reduce the need for complex high-order boundary derivatives during construction. As a result, the method maintains high-order accuracy while significantly improving computational efficiency for multi-dimensional problems. Finally, the stability of the proposed method is theoretically validated through linear stability analysis, and the effectiveness and robustness of the proposed scheme are numerically verified through a series of one-dimensional and two-dimensional numerical experiments for scalar and system equations.

### [10] [A Local Macroscopic Conservative Low-Rank Discontinuous Galerkin Method for the Vlasov-Poisson Equation with Dougherty-Fokker-Planck Collisions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19264)
*Austin Nelson,Wei Guo,Pierson Guthrey*

Main category: math.NA

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当库仑碰撞发生在稠密或弱碰撞等离子体中时，电子会被推向低秩稳态，且该稳态往往快速达到，导致大部分运行时间内等离子体主要由数值低秩结构组成。现有的方法未充分利用这一低秩特性来降低存储开销。

Method: 将库仑碰撞引入先前建立的LoMaC（局部宏观守恒）方法框架，构造低秩、保结构的DG方法。该方法利用等离子体中的数值低秩结构，在离散层面上保持宏观质量、动量和能量的局部守恒性。

Result: 通过数值实验验证了所提方法的有效性，表明该方法能在保持保结构特性的同时，显著降低VP-DFP系统模拟所需的存储复杂度。

Conclusion: 所构造的低秩LoMaC-DG方法能够有效处理带碰撞的VP系统，在保证宏观守恒量的前提下大幅降低存储需求，适用于稠密或弱碰撞等离子体中的长期模拟。

Abstract: In this paper, we construct a low-rank, structure preserving discontinuous Galerkin (DG) method to simulate the Vlasov-Poisson (VP) system coupled with the Dougherty Fokker-Planck (DFP) collision operator. When Coulomb collisions occur in dense or weakly-collisional plasmas, electrons get pushed to a low-rank steady state. In many cases, the plasma arrives to this steady state quickly, meaning that for most of the run-time, the plasma consists mainly of numerical low-rank structures. Our new low-rank scheme is constructed to exploit these numerical low-rank structures to greatly reduce the needed storage complexity of simulations for the VP-DFP system. It is constructed as an extension of the previously established Local Macroscopic Conservative (LoMaC) method by incorporating Coulomb collisions into the system. The LoMaC property ensures local conservation of macroscopic mass, momentum, and energy at the discrete level. Details of the new method are discussed in this paper. Numerical experiments are performed to show the efficacy of the method.

### [11] [Nyström Error Beyond $M$-Matrices: A Minimal Diagonally Dominant Obstruction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19282)
*Matthew J. Colbrook*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 本文研究了列选择的Nyström近似对核范数误差是否具有递减收益，证明了SDDM矩阵类在维度3时存在失败区间，严格对角占优时最小维度为4，并给出了符号三角形导致失败的公式化解释，完整回答了Simons研讨会报告中的问题4.6。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 核心问题是：对于由对称对角占优矩阵L诱导的核矩阵K的Nyström近似，其核范数误差是否具有递减收益（diminishing returns）性质。这是Simons研讨会报告Problem 4.6提出的开放问题。

Method: 1. 利用Schur补恒等式将问题转化为主子矩阵逆的迹问题；2. 对SDDM矩阵类利用现有M-矩阵结论解决；3. 构造精确的单参数SDD族并确定其严格失败区间；4. 利用2×2恒等式证明SDD类中维度3是最小失败维度；5. 证明严格对角占优下失败仍存在，且非空选定基集时最小失败维度为4；6. 证明符号切换不变性，推导三维公式说明有符号三角形导致失败；7. 给出贪婪列选择错过最优对的实例。

Result: 1. 对角占优（DD）本身不足以保证递减收益，在维度3即出现反例；2. SDDM矩阵类可保证递减收益；3. 构造了精确的单参数SDD族并确定了失败区间；4. 严格对角占优（SDD）下失败仍然存在，且当选定基集非空时最小失败维度为4；5. 符号切换不变性成立；6. 有符号三角形（signed triangle）是导致失败的结构性原因；7. 贪婪列选择可能无法找到最优列对。

Conclusion: 本文完整回答了Simons研讨会报告中的Problem 4.6，揭示了递减收益性质在SDD类中的边界条件和失败机制，对理解Nyström近似的误差行为具有重要理论意义。

Abstract: We study the nuclear-norm error of a column-selected Nyström approximation to $K=(L+γI)^{-1}$, where $L$ is symmetric diagonally dominant and $γ>0$. Our central question is whether this error has diminishing returns. A Schur-complement identity reduces the question to traces of inverses of principal submatrices. Existing $M$-matrix results settle the case in which $L$ is a symmetric diagonally dominant $M$-matrix (SDDM). However, diagonal dominance alone is not enough: failure occurs already in dimension three. We construct an exact one-parameter SDD family and determine its sharp failure interval. A $2\times2$ identity proves that dimension three is minimal within the SDD class. We then show that failure persists under strict diagonal dominance; with a nonempty selected base set, dimension four is minimal. Finally, we prove invariance under signature switching, derive a three-dimensional formula showing how a signed triangle causes failure, and give an example in which greedy column selection misses the optimal pair. Together, these findings complete the answer to Problem 4.6 in a recent Simons workshop report.

### [12] [1-Lipschitz Neural Networks on Hadamard Manifolds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19335)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 控制神经网络的Lipschitz常数是提升鲁棒性和稳定性的标准方法，但现有约束策略主要针对欧氏空间设计，缺乏适用于非欧几何流形（如Hadamard流形）的Lipschitz网络构造方法。

Method: 基于Busemann函数及其梯度流，构造了一类梯度下降类型的1-Lipschitz层，该层同时满足拟α-强非扩张性。在双曲流形和SPD矩阵流形上给出了显式构造和实例，并设计了几何保持的层结构。

Result: 在Poincaré圆盘上的鲁棒分类实验中，所提网络在双曲扰动下表现出鲁棒性；在SPD流形上的掩蔽Wishart协方差重建任务中，非扩张去噪器优于静态、纯数据及Log-Euclidean去噪基线，并验证了收敛性。

Abstract: Controlling the Lipschitz constant of a neural network is a standard way to promote robustness and stability. Most existing constraining strategies are designed for Euclidean spaces. In this work, we construct and analyze a class of 1-Lipschitz neural networks on Hadamard manifolds. Our layers are of gradient-descent type, $1$-Lipschitz, and quasi-$α$-firmly nonexpansive. The core building blocks of the proposed architecture are Busemann functions, and we exploit the properties of Busemann gradient flows to design $1$-Lipschitz geometry-preserving layers. We provide explicit constructions and examples for hyperbolic manifolds and the manifold of symmetric positive definite (SPD) matrices. We test the proposed architecture in two numerical experiments: robust classification on the Poincaré disk and masked-Wishart covariance reconstruction. On the Poincaré disk, the proposed networks yield robust classifiers under hyperbolic perturbations. On the SPD manifold, we train SPD-valued denoisers and adopt them as a Plug-and-Play prior for a masked-Wishart covariance reconstruction problem. We show improved results from the nonexpansive denoiser over static, data-only, and Log-Euclidean denoising baselines, and empirically test its convergence properties.

### [13] [Experimental and model-assisted analysis of lamella thinning and breakup in diesel-surrogate fuel-droplet wall impingement under Leidenfrost conditions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18324)
*Xinquan Liang,Daniel Olufemi Olurotimi,Xi Liu,Minghui Xu,Yuhao Xu*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 本研究通过实验和模型分析，探究了正十六烷单液滴在300-500°C热钢壁上的铺展与破碎行为（We数5.77-208.61），发现Leidenfrost状态下（350-500°C）的薄层-边缘模型能有效预测破碎前的铺展轨迹，且模型推断的薄层厚度（0.010-0.017初始液滴直径）可为热壁燃油液滴撞击模型提供局部状态信息，补充传统We数和温度分区图。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 柴油喷雾-壁面系统中，热壁燃油液滴撞击影响液体再分布、二次液滴形成及蒸发，但现有研究对高温下液滴铺展与破碎机制的定量预测能力不足，尤其缺乏对薄层状态与破碎时刻关系的深入理解。

Method: 实验采用高速背光成像记录单滴正十六烷撞击加热不锈钢壁的过程，分类沉积、反弹、喷射、破碎和飞溅等模态，测量铺展因子历史，并与薄层-边缘模型对比，评估模型预测能力，并反推破碎时刻的薄层厚度。

Result: 300°C未进入Leidenfrost状态，实验与模型偏差较大；350-500°C的Leidenfrost状态下，模型能较好捕捉破碎前铺展轨迹；壁温对早期铺展影响有限，但对破碎时刻影响显著；高We下破碎由惯性主导；模型反推的破碎时刻薄层厚度集中在0.010-0.017初始液滴直径。

Conclusion: 模型推断的薄层厚度可提供局部状态信息，用于预测破碎时机，补充传统We数和温度分区图，为热壁燃油液滴撞击模型提供更精确的建模依据。

Abstract: Hot-wall fuel-droplet impingement affects liquid redistribution, secondary droplet formation, and droplet evaporation in diesel-relevant spray-wall systems. This study investigates the spreading and breakup of single n-hexadecane droplets, used as a single-component diesel surrogate, on a heated stainless-steel wall at 300-500 °C over a Weber number (We) range of 5.77-208.61. High-speed backlit images were recorded during experiments and used to classify deposition, rebound, ejection, fragmentation, and splashing regimes, and to measure spreading-factor histories. The measured spreading histories were compared with a lamella-rim model to evaluate its predictive capability before droplet breakup and to infer the lamella state at experimentally observed breakup instants. The 300 °C cases did not enter the Leidenfrost regime under the present impact conditions and therefore serve as a non-Leidenfrost reference, deviating from the model predictions. For Leidenfrost cases at 350-500 °C, the model captures the pre-breakup spreading trajectory, including higher-We cases that later undergo breakup. Wall temperature has a limited influence on the early spreading stage but more strongly affects later breakup timing after lamella thinning, especially in the intermediate-We regime. At high We, breakup becomes increasingly inertia-dominated. Model-inferred lamella thicknesses evaluated at experimentally observed breakup instants are mainly concentrated between 0.010 and 0.017 of the initial droplet diameter. These results suggest that model-inferred lamella thickness can complement conventional Weber-number and temperature-based regime maps by providing local-state information for breakup timing in hot-wall fuel-droplet impingement models.

### [14] [Spontaneous stochasticity and anomalous dissipation in collapsing wave turbulence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18788)
*Wandrille Ruffenach*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 本文研究了聚焦型Majda–McLaughlin–Tabak方程在有限时间波塌缩后的非唯一性后爆破解，发现粘性正则化与非线性和饱和正则化在塌缩后给出不同的极限，且均无法唯一选择解，表现出自发随机性特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究聚焦型MMT方程在有限时间波塌缩后经典解终结、出现无穷多解的非唯一性后爆破区间，以及不同正则化方案在该区间的行为差异。

Method: 采用两种正则化方案（粘性扩散和非线性和饱和）分别避免爆破，研究对应的消失正则化极限，并分析参数与小扰动的敏感性。

Result: 两种正则化在塌缩前收敛到同一光滑无粘解，但在塌缩后极限不同：粘性近似出现反常质量耗散，饱和近似保持保守；两者均无法唯一选择后爆破解，参数或初值的小扰动会在奇异极限后产生有限后爆破不确定性。

Conclusion: 塌缩波湍流属于自发随机性范畴，无粘极限更适合用概率分布而非确定解描述；尺度逐层涨落预算表明塌缩事件是不确定性产生的局域源；该现象不仅限于流体湍流，也可推广至色散介质体系。

Abstract: We study a focusing Majda--McLaughlin--Tabak type equation undergoing finite-time wave collapse. This singularity terminates the classical smooth solution and opens a post-blowup regime where infinitely many solutions may exist. To probe this nonunique regime, we regularize the dynamics either by viscous diffusion or by nonlinear saturation and study the corresponding vanishing-regularization limits. Both regularizations prevent blowup at fixed parameter and recover the same inviscid collapse as the parameter vanishes. Before collapse, they converge to the same smooth inviscid solution. After collapse, however, their limits differ. The viscous approximation undergoes anomalous mass dissipation whereas the saturating approximation remains conservative. Moreover, neither regularization selects a unique post-blowup solution. Vanishing perturbations of the regularization parameter or of the initial condition survive the singular limit and generate finite post-blowup uncertainty. This places collapsing wave turbulence in the setting of spontaneous stochasticity, where the inviscid limit is better described in terms probability law on inviscid solutions rather than deterministically. Scale-by-scale fluctuation budgets identify collapse events as localized sources of uncertainty production. While spontaneous stochasticity is usually associated with fluid turbulence, these results provide numerical evidence that it can be applied to a broader class of systems, including dispersive media in which experiments could be conducted.

</details>


### [15] [Preferential and differential diffusion in RANS simulation of lean hydrogen flames with tabulated chemistry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18993)
*Alex M. Garcia,Emiliano M. Fortes,Eduardo J. Pérez-Sánchez,Daniel Mira,Marco Vivenzo,Michael Gauding,Heinz Pitsch,Nico Schmitz,Christian Wuppermann*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于从考虑混合平均扩散和Soret效应的物种质量输运方程推导的进度变量和混合分数输运方程，采用假定概率密度函数方法处理湍流-化学反应相互作用，将包含优先和差异扩散的TC模型扩展到RANS框架。

Conclusion: 该模型能够在计算成本较低的RANS模拟中有效包含优先和差异扩散效应，适用于贫燃氢气火焰的工程模拟。

Abstract: Lean hydrogen flames are prone to thermo-diffusive instabilities due to preferential and differential diffusion effects, posing significant challenges for their modeling in computational fluid dynamics simulations. This work extends a tabulated-chemistry (TC) model that includes preferential and differential diffusion effects to a Reynolds-averaged Navier-Stokes (RANS) framework and assesses its performance for a lean premixed $\mathrm{H_2}$-air slot burner at two Reynolds numbers ($\mathrm{Re}=5500$ and $11000$) using direct numerical simulation (DNS) as a reference. The approach is based on transport equations for the progress variable and mixture fraction derived from the species mass transport equations considering mixture-averaged diffusion and Soret effect, and incorporates turbulence--chemistry interaction via a presumed probability density function (PDF) approach. RANS simulations including preferential-differential diffusion are able to correctly reproduce the DNS flame length, heat-release distribution, and the characteristic equivalence-ratio and super-adiabatic temperature branches of the slot flame. Comparisons with (i) a unity-Lewis-number variant and (ii) a model including thermo-diffusive effects only in the flamelet table show the impact of preferential and differential diffusion on the TC model at both the thermochemical and transport levels. Finally, the impact of the turbulence closures for turbulent diffusion, scalar dissipation rate, and Reynolds stresses is assessed. The results presented in this paper demonstrate the capability of the model to include preferential and differential diffusion effects in cost-effective RANS simulations of lean hydrogen flames.

### [16] [Long rigid fibres in a turbulent channel flow: comparison between experiments and simulations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19116)
*Defa Sun,Florian Zumbo,Christophe Pitiot,Sandra Bosio,Cyrille Claudet,Jeremie Bec,Christophe Brouzet*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 本文通过实验和数值模拟研究了湍流槽道中长刚性纤维的动力学行为，考察了纤维长度（ℓ/h=0.25, 0.5, 1）和壁面约束对平移、取向和翻转运动的影响。研究发现：近壁区最短纤维快于局部平均流而长纤维更慢；取向统计在壁面距离用纤维长度归一化后呈现普适性塌缩；"pole-vaulting"事件导致局部翻转率峰值出现在y⁺≈ℓ⁺/2处，其幅度与(ℓ⁺)⁻²成正比。实验与模拟在取向和翻转上吻合较好，但在平移速度上存在差异，反映了沉降、有限纤维厚度和有限滑移雷诺数的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解湍流中长刚性纤维的动力学行为，特别是纤维长度和壁面约束对纤维平移、取向和翻转运动的影响机制，以及近壁区纤维与湍流相互作用的物理规律。

Method: 实验采用三种长度（ℓ/h=0.25, 0.5, 1）的聚苯乙烯纤维（惯性St⁺≈20），在湍流槽道中进行测量，并与基于刚性细长体模型的数值模拟进行系统对比。采用基于壁面距离条件统计的方法分析纤维行为。

Result: 1) 远离壁面时纤维滞后于流体，速度亏损与长度无明显依赖关系；2) 近壁区最短纤维快于局部平均流，长纤维仍较慢；3) 近壁纤维主要进行"kayaking"运动（在近似平行于壁面的平面内翻转）；4) 取向统计在y⁺/ℓ⁺归一化后塌缩；5) "pole-vaulting"事件产生局部翻转率峰值在y⁺≈ℓ⁺/2处，幅度与(ℓ⁺)⁻²成正比。

Conclusion: 壁面距离用纤维长度归一化（y⁺/ℓ⁺）是描述近壁纤维取向统计的关键几何变量；实验与模拟在取向和翻转上一致性良好，但平移速度的差异表明模型未能完全反映沉降、有限纤维厚度和有限滑移雷诺数的影响。

Abstract: The dynamics of long rigid fibres transported by turbulent channel flow are investigated experimentally and numerically. Experiments use polystyrene fibres of three lengths, $\ell/h=0.25$, $0.5$ and $1$, with moderate inertia, $St^+\approx20$. Their settling velocity is comparable to the friction velocity, causing accumulation near the bottom wall. Measurements are compared systematically with simulations based on a rigid slender-body model. Statistics conditioned on the distance from the wall are used to characterise the effects of fibre length and confinement on translation, orientation and tumbling. Away from the wall, the experimental fibres lag the fluid, with no clear dependence of the velocity deficit on length. Near the wall, the shortest fibres move faster than the local mean flow, whereas longer fibres remain slower, indicating length-dependent sampling of near-wall turbulence. Confinement also strongly constrains orientation and rotation. Fibres close to the wall predominantly undergo "kayaking" motion, tumbling in planes approximately parallel to it. Orientation statistics collapse when wall distance is normalised by fibre length, identifying $y^+/\ell^+$ as the relevant geometrical variable. Where fibres can acquire a significant wall-normal orientation, "pole-vaulting" events produce a local tumbling-rate maximum at $y^+\approx\ell^+/2$. Its magnitude decreases approximately as $(\ell^+)^{-2}$, consistently with a dimensional estimate based on the near-wall velocity variation sampled along the fibre. Experiments and simulations agree well for orientation and tumbling but differ more for translational velocity. The discrepancies highlight the effect of settling, finite fibre thickness and finite slip Reynolds number that are not fully represented by the model.

</details>

### [17] [Information Compression at Criticality](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18388)
*Simon Jiricek,Miroslav Hopjan,Boris Altshuler,Vladimir Kravtsov,Lev Vidmar*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文揭示了处于临界性边界的高度激发量子态，通过能量空间中的信息压缩方法，发现哈密顿谱可以被系统性地截断，仅用极少部分本征能级即可重现生存概率的幂律衰减行为，截断谱表现出分形结构，其能级间距分布和谱形因子均具有幂律尾部特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解处于遍历性临界边界的激发量子态的动力学性质，这些状态偏离热行为但其动力学特性尚不清楚。

Method: 通过能量空间中的内在信息压缩视角，对哈密顿谱进行系统性截断，研究截断后的简化描述对动力学核心特征的保留能力，分析能级间距分布与谱形因子的标度行为。

Result: 无论相互作用系统还是非相互作用系统，极少数（趋于零的比例）的哈密顿本征能级就足以再现生存概率的幂律衰减；截断谱呈现分形结构，能级间距分布具有幂律尾部，且谱形因子与生存概率具有相同的渐近幂律衰减行为。

Conclusion: 临界系统哈密顿谱存在内在的可压缩性，其动力学本质由少部分能级的分形结构主导，提供了从信息压缩角度理解非遍历性量子动力学的新视角。

Abstract: Highly excited quantum states at the critical boundary of ergodicity are known to deviate from thermal behavior, yet their dynamical properties remain poorly understood. Here, we uncover the complexity of quantum dynamics at criticality through the lens of intrinsic information compression in energy space. We show that the Hamiltonian spectrum can be systematically truncated, yielding a simplified description of the dynamics while preserving its essential features. Specifically, for both interacting and noninteracting systems, we demonstrate that a vanishing fraction of Hamiltonian eigenlevels suffices to reproduce the power-law decay of the survival probability. The resulting truncated spectrum exhibits a fractal structure characterized by a level-spacing distribution with a power-law tail, while its spectral form factor displays the same asymptotic power-law decay as the survival probability.

</details>


### [18] [Absence of hidden analytic conserved quantities in harmonically confined rods](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18872)
*Sahil Kumar Singh,Abhishek Dhar,Sanjay Moudgalya*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文严格证明了在简谐势阱中长度非零的硬杆系统不存在除总能和质心能之外的解析守恒量，并通过自由运动时的U(1)对称性和碰撞时的S_N对称性推导出这一结论；同时指出当杆长度为零（点粒子）时存在大量额外的解析守恒量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 硬杆系统在简谐势阱中表现出非遍历行为，暗示可能存在未知的守恒量。本文旨在严格检验这一猜想，系统性地约束守恒量的形式，以确定是否存在额外的隐藏守恒量。

Method: 采用对称性分析方法：从守恒量在自由运动下的条件推导出U(1)不变性（旋转每个杆的位置和动量）；从碰撞条件推导出S_N不变性（在至少一根杆长度非零时，杆的动量置换不变）。结合这两个条件证明任何解析守恒量都只能依赖于已知的两个守恒量。

Result: 1. 长度非零的硬杆系统不存在任何额外的解析守恒量；2. 点粒子极限下（杆长为零），碰撞条件仅需更小的S_N标签置换群不变性，由此可显式写出大量额外的解析守恒量。

Conclusion: 本文严格澄清了一维简谐势阱中硬杆系统守恒量的结构，证明了非遍历行为并非源于隐藏守恒量，并为其他经典系统中守恒量的系统性分析方法提供了启发。

Abstract: Systems of hard rods of equal length in a one-dimensional harmonic trap have been observed to exhibit peculiar non-ergodic behavior that might suggest the existence of a novel hidden conserved quantity beyond the two well known ones, i.e., the total energy and the center-of-mass energy. In this work, we investigate this possibility by systematically constraining the forms of the conserved quantities, and we rigorously rule out the existence of any extra hidden conserved quantity that is analytic in the positions and momenta of the rods involved. We do so by showing two key results: conservation during free motion demands the $U(1)$ invariance of these quantities under rotations of the position and momenta of each rod, and conservation during collisions demand an $S_N$ invariance under the permutation of the momenta of the rods as long as one of the rods have non-zero length. We then show that these conditions imply that any conserved quantity is functionally dependent on the two known conserved quantities. In addition, we show that in the special case where all rods have zero length (i.e., when they are point particles), conservation under collisions only requires invariance under a smaller $S_N$ group of permutations of the labels of the rods, which leads to a much larger set of analytic conserved quantities that we explicitly write down. In all, this rigorously clarifies the structure of conserved quantities in the hard rod problem, and motivates the application of such systematic methods to other classical systems.

</details>


### [19] [Deterministic cascade coarsening in a Bistable Gene Toggle model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18891)
*Priyanka D. Bhoyar,Prashant M. Gade*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究双稳态基因拨动模型中的确定性粗化动力学，发现了一种不同于经典曲率驱动粗化的新机制：畴壁长时间钉扎后通过级联事件突然消失，粗化呈现对数周期振荡，且衰减指数δ<0.5，偏离Allen-Cahn预言。对数周期振荡由级联中消失的畴控制，其平均尺寸随级联指数线性增长，符合离散尺度不变性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典曲率驱动粗化理论（Allen-Cahn预言δ=1/2）在双稳态基因拨动模型中是否仍然成立？探索新型粗化机制的物理起源。

Method: 对具有扩散耦合的空间扩展双稳态基因拨动模型进行确定性粗化动力学数值模拟，分析畴壁密度衰减、对数周期振荡特征及级联事件统计规律。

Result: 畴壁密度衰减指数δ<0.5，偏离经典1/2；粗化呈现对数周期振荡；振荡由级联中消失的畴控制，其平均尺寸随级联指数线性增长。

Conclusion: 该系统中粗化动力学由离散尺度不变性主导，不同于经典连续曲率驱动粗化，揭示了双稳态基因调控网络中一种新的时空有序化机制。

Abstract: We investigate deterministic coarsening dynamics in a spatially extended bistable gene toggle model with diffusive coupling. Unlike classical curvature-driven coarsening, where domain walls move continuously and annihilate gradually, the present system exhibits a qualitatively different mechanism. The domain walls remain pinned for long intervals and disappear abruptly through collective cascade events. The density of domain walls decays approximately as $ρ(t)\sim t^{-δ}$, but the coarsening exhibits clear log-periodic oscillations superimposed on the power-law behavior. For all values of the promoter strength $α$ considered, the measured exponent satisfies $δ<0.5$, indicating a systematic deviation from the classical Allen--Cahn prediction $δ=1/2$ for curvature-driven coarsening. We show that log-periodic oscillations are not controlled by the density of domain walls, but by the \emph{domains that disappear} in each cascade. The average size of disappearing domains grows roughly linearly with cascade index, producing a constant geometric spacing of cascade times, consistent with discrete scale invariance.

</details>


### [20] [Energy Conversion, Fluctuation Suppression, and Information Transfer in the Thermodynamic Performance of Kinesin](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18905)
*Riku Kato,Takayuki Ariga,Tomohiro Tanogami*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本研究构建了一个热力学一致的双态驱动蛋白-货物模型，系统比较了多种热力学效率（热力学效率、信息-热力学效率、TUR效率和二分TUR效率），发现这些效率普遍较低，表明驱动蛋白并非为最大化这些热力学效率而优化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有研究使用随机热力学框架下的不同效率指标量化驱动蛋白性能，但由于模型和假设各异，难以进行定量比较，导致不清楚驱动蛋白在哪个方面（如果有）是热力学优化的。

Method: 构建了一个热力学一致的双态驱动蛋白-货物模型，保留了驱动蛋白的离散步进及其与货物的耦合；假设马达与货物之间存在时间尺度分离，推导了热力学效率、信息-热力学效率、TUR效率和二分TUR效率的解析表达式，并与数值模拟结果进行比较。

Result: 所考察的多种热力学效率普遍较低，表明驱动蛋白并非为最大化这些效率而优化。

Conclusion: 热力学效率本身可能不足以完全表征驱动蛋白性能，需要进一步从互补的动力学视角评估分子马达功能。

Abstract: Kinesin is a molecular motor that transports intracellular cargoes along microtubules. Recent studies have quantified kinesin performance using various efficiencies within the framework of stochastic thermodynamics; however, quantitative comparisons remain difficult because different models and assumptions have been employed. As a result, it remains unclear which aspect of kinesin performance, if any, is thermodynamically optimized. Here, we systematically compare multiple thermodynamic efficiencies within a single kinesin-cargo model. To this end, we construct a thermodynamically consistent two-state kinesin-cargo model that retains both the discrete stepping of kinesin and its coupling to the cargo. Assuming a separation of time scales between the motor and the cargo, we derive analytical expressions for the thermodynamic efficiency, the information-thermodynamic efficiency, the thermodynamic uncertainty relation (TUR) efficiency, and the bipartite TUR efficiency, and compare them with numerical simulation results. We find that these efficiencies generally remain low, suggesting that kinesin is not optimized for maximizing the thermodynamic efficiencies considered here. Our results suggest that thermodynamic efficiencies alone may not fully characterize kinesin performance and motivate further investigation of complementary kinetic perspectives for assessing molecular motor function.

### [21] [Discrete distributions and statistical mechanics of small systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18968)
*Lev B. Klebanov,Michal Šumbera*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究了离散概率分布与小系统统计力学之间的联系，利用概率生成函数发展了非负整数值随机变量的幂级数、无穷可分和可缩放分布理论，并引入马尔可夫分布类。这些结果应用于统计力学的巨正则系综描述，提出了液-气相变动力学模型，并展示了在Tsallis非广延热力学中可缩放性的保持以及变形离散分布的自然出现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 建立离散概率分布理论与小系统统计力学之间的形式化联系，为理解相互作用气体的准粒子图像、液-气相变的临界行为以及非广延热力学中的分布特征提供统一的数学框架。

Method: 利用概率生成函数作为核心工具，发展幂级数分布、无穷可分分布和可缩放分布的理论体系；引入马尔可夫分布类（生灭过程的平稳解）；应用巨正则系综描述建立组合子与维里展开的联系；通过重正化半群变换分析临界点离散稳定分布；在Tsallis非广延热力学框架下检验可缩放性。

Result: 1) 无穷可分性导致相互作用气体的准粒子图像；2) 维里展开与分布的组合子建立联系；3) 液-气相变临界点的粒子数分布收敛到离散稳定分布（重正化半群变换的不动点）；4) Tsallis非广延热力学中可缩放性保持但无穷可分性失效；5) 负二项分布作为泊松分布的q-变形自然出现。

Conclusion: 离散概率分布理论为统计力学中的若干核心问题提供了新的数学视角，从经典系综到非广延热力学均有统一的形式化刻画，特别是在临界现象和变形分布方面展现了理论潜力。

Abstract: We study connections between discrete probability distributions and the statistical mechanics of small systems. Using probability generating functions, we develop the theory of power series, infinitely divisible, and scalable distributions of non-negative integer-valued random variables, and introduce the class of Markovian distributions that arise naturally in stationary solutions of birth-death processes and in scalable infinitely divisible distributions.
  These results are applied to the grand canonical ensemble description in statistical mechanics: the infinite divisibility leads to a quasiparticle picture of an interacting gas, and the virial expansion is linked to the combinants of the distribution. A kinetic model of the liquid-vapor phase transition is presented, in which the particle-number distribution at the critical point converges to the Discrete Stable distribution - the fixed point of a renormalization semi-group transformation. We also show that the scalability of the particle-number distribution is preserved in Tsallis non-extensive thermodynamics, even though infinite divisibility fails. Moreover, deformed discrete distributions, including the negative binomial as a q-deformation of the Poisson, arise naturally in this setting.

</details>


### [22] [Boundary quenches in (1+1)-dimensional conformal field theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19166)
*Michele Fossati,Colin Rylands,Eytan Grosfeld,Eran Sela,Pasquale Calabrese*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究(1+1)维共形场论中边界条件突然改变所引起的局域量子淬火，导出了半直线上单点函数时间演化的普适表达式，发现当子系统与淬火事件完全因果连接时，纠缠熵会发生一个尖锐的有限跳变，其大小由初始和最终边界条件的g因子比值的对数决定。通过临界伊辛自旋链的矩阵乘积态模拟验证了理论预测，并进一步研究了自旋翻转纠缠不对称性的时间演化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究对边界量子淬火中纠缠动力学的普适性理解尚不充分，特别是缺乏对边界条件突变后纠缠熵演化的精确解析描述。本文旨在揭示边界淬火中纠缠动力学的普适标度行为，并建立非平衡纠缠动力学与边界临界现象之间的直接联系。

Method: 采用(1+1)维共形场论分析框架，通过边界共形场论方法推导单点函数的时间演化；结合量子淬火情景，利用因果传播图像分析纠缠熵动力学；通过临界伊辛自旋链的矩阵乘积态(MPS)数值模拟进行理论验证，并计算自旋翻转纠缠不对称性。

Result: 导出了单点函数时间演化的简单普适表达式；发现子系统完全因果连接到淬火事件时，纠缠熵发生尖锐有限跳变，跳变幅度由初始与最终边界g因子比值的对数给出。MPS模拟结果与理论预测高度吻合。自旋翻转纠缠不对称性揭示了对称性破缺扰动从边界向体相的传播过程。

Conclusion: 本文揭示了边界淬火中纠缠动力学的普适动力学特征，建立了非平衡纠缠动力学与边界临界现象之间的直接联系，为理解边界量子淬火提供了统一的解析框架。

Abstract: We investigate a class of local quantum quenches in which the conformal boundary condition of a (1+1)-dimensional conformal field theory is abruptly changed. We derive a remarkably simple and universal expression for the time evolution of one-point functions on the half-line. This result provides a direct description of the propagation of the disturbance generated by the quench and, in turn, allows us to determine the dynamics of bipartite entanglement for subsystems adjacent to the boundary. We show that, once the subsystem becomes fully causally connected to the quench event, the entanglement entropy undergoes a sharp finite jump whose magnitude is universally given by the logarithm of the ratio of the boundary g-factors associated with the initial and final boundary conditions. We benchmark these analytical predictions against Matrix Product State simulations of the critical Ising spin chain, finding excellent agreement. The numerical analysis further allows us to investigate the time evolution of the spin-flip entanglement asymmetry, revealing how the symmetry-breaking perturbation emitted from the boundary propagates through the system. Our results uncover universal dynamical signatures of boundary quenches and establish a direct connection between nonequilibrium entanglement dynamics and boundary critical phenomena.

</details>


### [23] [Dynamical correlation functions of extensive charges after global quantum quenches](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19208)
*Riccardo Travaglino,Katja Klobas,Bruno Bertini,Pasquale Calabrese*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究了量子淬火后U(1)电荷的n次累积量生成函数（n-FCS），利用时空对偶性，证明了在弱时间关联（如弹道输运）条件下，n-FCS可分解为时间壳结构内的单时FCS之和，并指出该结构导致动力学关联函数在时间排序下仅依赖于最小时间。通过自由和相互作用模型的解析与数值验证支持了这些结论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解量子淬火后多体系统中U(1)电荷的涨落统计（特别是高阶累积量），并揭示其时域关联结构对动力学关联函数的简化作用。

Method: 利用时空对偶性（space-time duality）分析对称初始态下的n-FCS，通过分解为单时FCS的时间壳结构，结合解析推导和数值模拟（自由及相互作用模型）验证理论预测。

Result: 在弱时间关联（如弹道输运）条件下，n-FCS因子化为单时FCS的时间壳求和；动力学关联函数在时间排序下仅依赖于最小时间。

Conclusion: 时空对偶性为分析量子淬火后电荷涨落提供了有效框架，揭示了时间关联弱化时高阶统计量的简化结构，对理解非平衡多体系统的关联函数具有重要意义。

Abstract: We investigate the $n$-time cumulant generating function (or $n$-Full Counting Statistics, $n$-FCS) of extensive $U(1)$ charges following a quantum quench. Exploiting space-time duality we characterise this function when evolving from initial states that are symmetric under the action of the charge. In particular, we show that if the correlations in time are sufficiently weak, e.g.\ the transport is ballistic, the $n$-FCS factorises into a sum of single-time FCS arranged in a time-shell structure. A direct implication of this structure is a drastic simplification of dynamical correlation functions: in the presence of time ordering they only depend on the smallest time entering the correlator. We support these findings with several analytical and numerical tests performed in free and interacting models.

</details>


### [24] [Statistical properties of quadrangular surfaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19221)
*Hrant Topchyan,Rudik Badalyan,Ara Sedrakyan*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究了三种随机四边曲面（GKNS、DQ、GQ）的统计性质。GKNS等价于两个相互约束的逾渗过程，具有宽尺度无标度度分布和约2的Hausdorff维数；DQ和GQ则表现出不同的几何行为，其中DQ与DT普适类相容，GQ定义了新的随机几何类，暗示随机曲面空间中存在不同的测度，可能为新型非临界弦理论提供几何框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随机曲面的统计性质是理解量子引力和弦理论的重要途径。已有研究关注了不同的随机曲面生成过程（如GKNS构造和DT），但对它们的统计特性及其相互关系的统一理解仍然缺乏。本文旨在系统比较三种随机四边曲面过程，揭示它们本质上的几何差异性，并探索新的随机几何类。

Method: 采用统一图论框架将三种随机曲面（GKNS、DQ、GQ）形式化。证明GKNS等价于两个相互约束的逾渗过程，并计算其临界点和临界指数；对DQ和GQ分析底层马尔可夫链，标度混合时间和弛豫时间；通过度分布、度关联、距离统计和Hausdorff维数全面分析三种系综的几何性质。

Result: GKNS具有宽尺度无标度度分布，渐近Hausdorff维数约2；DQ具有指数衰减度分布，Hausdorff维数约4，与DT相容；GQ同样具有宽尺度度分布，Hausdorff维数约4，但定义了与DT不同的随机几何类。

Conclusion: 三种随机曲面过程属于不同的随机几何类：DQ与DT（动力三角剖分）普适类相容，而GKNS和GQ定义了不同的随机几何测度，这可能为新型非临界弦理论提供几何框架。

Abstract: We investigate the statistical properties of random quadrangular surfaces generated by different randomization procedures: the Gruzberg-Klümper-Nuding-Sedrakyan (GKNS) construction, and two newly introduced generalizations of dynamical triangulations (DT), dynamical (DQ) and general quadrangulations (GQ). We formulate these surfaces within a unified graph-theoretic framework and establish the relationships between the elementary operations defining the different ensembles. For GKNS surfaces, we demonstrate that the construction is equivalent to two mutually constrained percolation processes and determine the associated critical point and critical exponents, revealing deviations from ordinary percolation. For DQ and GQ, we analyze the underlying Markov chains and determine the scaling of mixing and relaxation times. We further analyze all three ensembles through their degree distributions, degree correlations, distance statistics, and Hausdorff dimensions. While DQ exhibits exponentially decaying degree distributions and geometric properties similar to DT, GKNS and GQ display broad, scale-free degree distributions. Moreover, GKNS surfaces possess an asymptotic Hausdorff dimension $Δ_H\approx 2$, whereas DQ and GQ approach $Δ_H\approx 4$, similarly to DT. This indicates that DQ is compatible with the universal behavior of DT, while GKNS and GQ define distinct classes of random geometry, implying a different underlying measure in the space of random surfaces and a possible geometric framework for a new class of noncritical string theories.

</details>

### [25] [Homogenization for the $p$-Laplacian in a $d$-dimensional ball perforated along the unit sphere: the critical case $p=d$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18487)
*Peter V. Gordon,Yuval Peres*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文研究了穿孔区域中p-Laplacian边值问题，在临界情况p=d>1下，通过参数τ识别临界尺度，发现解在远离单位球面处收敛于A*Uρ，其中A*依赖于τ的取值（0、∞或有限正值），并构造了在L∞和d-容量意义下逼近解的显式渐近形式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解穿孔区域中p-Laplacian方程的解在临界尺度下的渐近行为，特别是当孔洞分布在单位球面附近且其大小和间距由参数ε控制时的极限行为。

Method: 通过参数τ=lim[εlog(1/α(ε))]^{-1}识别临界尺度，构造显式渐近解，利用d-容量分析，研究解在L∞和容量意义下的收敛性。

Result: 解在远离单位球面处收敛于A*Uρ，其中Uρ为径向d-调和势；常数A*在τ=0时为0，τ=∞时为1，有限τ时有显式表达式；构造的渐近解在L∞和d-容量意义下对充分小的ε有效。

Conclusion: 在临界情况p=d下，孔洞的尺度与间距通过参数τ决定了宏观解的极限行为，从完全屏蔽（τ=0）到无屏蔽（τ=∞）存在连续过渡。

Abstract: We study a boundary value problem for the $p$-Laplacian in the perforated domain $B(0,ρ)\setminusΓ\subset \mathbb{R}^d$, where $ρ>1$ and $Γ$ is the union of many small compact cavities placed near the unit sphere. The cavities are separated at scale $\varepsilon$, asymptotically equidistributed on the sphere, and have cardinality of order $\varepsilon^{1-d}$. The cavities have diameters of order $α(\varepsilon)\varepsilon$, where $α(\varepsilon)\to0$, and their relative $p$-capacity is comparable to the relative p-capacity of a ball of the same diameter. The solution is required to equal $1$ on all cavities and $0$ on $\partial B(0,ρ)$. We focus on the critical case $p=d>1$.
  We identify the critical scale through the parameter $τ=\lim_{\varepsilon\downarrow0}[\varepsilon\log(1/α(\varepsilon))]^{-1}\in[0,\infty]$. Thus, $α(\varepsilon)=\exp[-(1+o(1))/(τ\varepsilon)]$ when $0<τ<\infty$. Away from the unit sphere, the solutions converge to $A_*U_ρ$, where $U_ρ(x)=\min\{1,1-\log |x|/\logρ\}$ is the radial $d$-harmonic potential of the unit ball in $B(0,ρ)$. The constant $A_*$ equals $0$ when $τ=0$, equals $1$ when $τ=\infty$, and is explicit for $0<τ<\infty$. We construct an explicit ansatz that approximates the solution for sufficiently small $\varepsilon$ in both $L^{\infty}$ and in terms of $d$-capacity.

</details>


### [26] [The Stefan problem for complete melting of finitely strained solids into viscoelastic fluids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18547)
*Tomáš Roubíček*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文在欧拉框架下建立了大应变可压缩流固相互作用（FSI）与热力学相变的理论模型，采用Jeffreys流变学处理偏应力部分，并通过温度依赖的粘性（或粘塑性）响应控制固-液相变，使材料在融化时完全退化为粘弹性流体，允许无限次冻融循环。经典Stefan问题通过引入动力学过热和过冷得到扩展，并利用多极非简单连续介质概念对高阶梯度修正公式进行时间离散截断分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 建立一种能够描述可压缩流固相互作用中伴随热力学相变（固-液相变）的大变形理论框架，使材料在融化后完全丧失弹性剪切响应以允许自由流动，并在凝固后恢复弹性，支持无限次冻融循环。

Method: 采用欧拉描述下的大应变框架，使用Jeffreys（反Zener）流变学结合附加粘度处理偏应力部分；通过温度依赖的粘性（或粘塑性）响应实现固-液相变的机械控制；利用多极非简单连续介质概念对原始公式进行高阶梯度修正，并采用含适当截断的时间离散化方法进行分析。

Result: 成功构建了可描述无限次冻融循环的流固相互作用理论模型，扩展了经典Stefan问题使其包含动力学过热和过冷效应，并通过高阶梯度修正和时间离散截断实现了理论公式的适定性分析。

Conclusion: 该理论为描述涉及相变（如冻融循环）的流固耦合问题提供了完整的数学框架，通过引入温度依赖的粘弹性退化机制，实现了从固态到液态的平滑过渡和逆过程，具有广泛的应用前景（如冰川动力学、材料加工等）。

Abstract: The compressible fluid-solid interaction (FSI) with a thermomechanical phase transition is formulated at large strains within the Eulerian frame. For the deviatoric part, the Jeffreys (also called anti-Zener) rheology with an additional viscosity is adopted. The core philosophy governing the mechanical solid-liquid transition is that the viscous (or viscoplastic) response is temperature-dependent and may fully degenerate to a viscoelastic fluid during thawing, so that there is no elastic response on the shear distortion. This behavior enables the free flow of the fluid, its subsequent freezing into a new configuration, and potential re-melting back into a fluid, allowing such cycles to repeat indefinitely. The classical Stefan problem, associated with the latent heat of the first-order (thawing-freezing) phase transition, is augmented by incorporating kinetic overheating and undercooling. The analysis by a time discretization with an appropriate truncation is applied to a higher-gradient modification of the original formulation, utilizing the concept of multipolar nonsimple continua.

</details>


### [27] [Delayed diffusion with measure-valued kernels in nonlinear parabolic equations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18610)
*Yuki Tsukamoto*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文研究具有延迟扩散项的非线性抛物方程，其中延迟核为有限符号测度。通过将原点处的原子吸收到当前时间算子中，剩余部分作为残余延迟核处理，在有效当前时间算子的结构假设和总记忆算子的路径 coercivity 条件下，证明了弱解的存在唯一性及其在核弱星收敛下的稳定性。稳定性结果涵盖了延迟原子坍缩（其质量在极限中转移到当前时间扩散系数）的情况。通过p-Laplacian类型例子验证了假设。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 处理带有延迟扩散项的非线性抛物方程，尤其是当延迟核包含原点原子（即瞬时部分）时的弱解存在唯一性及稳定性问题。

Method: 将原点处的原子吸收到当前时间算子中，将剩余部分视为残余延迟核；利用有效当前时间算子的结构假设和总记忆算子的路径 coercivity 条件进行理论分析。

Result: 在给定假设下证明了弱解的存在唯一性，并证明了在核弱星收敛意义下的稳定性，包括延迟原子坍缩到当前时间扩散系数的极限情形。

Conclusion: 所提出的分析框架有效处理了带有测度值延迟核的非线性抛物方程，并在p-Laplacian类型例子中得到验证。

Abstract: We study nonlinear parabolic equations with delayed diffusion terms governed by finite signed measure kernels. The atom of the kernel at the origin is absorbed into the present-time operator, while the remaining part is treated as a residual delay kernel. Under structural assumptions on the effective present-time operators and a pathwise coercivity condition for the total memory operator, we prove the existence and uniqueness of weak solutions and their stability under weak-star convergence of the kernels. The stability result covers collapsing delayed atoms, whose mass is transferred to the present-time diffusion coefficient in the limit. We verify the assumptions for p-Laplacian type examples, including separated kernels and a regularized class of kernels reaching the origin.

</details>


### [28] [Subsonic time-periodic solutions to radially symmetric spiral flows in an annulus](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18701)
*Huimin Yu,Zihao Zhang*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文研究环形区域内具有非零角速度的径向对称非等熵欧拉系统的亚音速时间周期解。在边界条件内圈耗散、外圈非耗散假设下，证明了接近稳态径向对称亚音速螺旋流的时间周期解的存在性与稳定性，且背景亚音速解无小量限制。关键方法是将熵的径向导数重写为沿第一或第四特征方向的导数，并通过适当限制环形宽度来控制沿特征曲线的扰动累积。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究环形区域内具有非零角速度的径向对称非等熵欧拉系统的时间周期解，解决背景亚音速解无小量限制下解的存在性与稳定性问题。

Method: 将熵的径向导数重写为沿第一或第四特征方向的导数，并通过对环形宽度施加适当限制来控制沿特征曲线的扰动累积，从而克服径向熵导数耦合导致的导数损失以及非零角速度引入的零阶项等困难。

Result: 建立了接近稳态径向对称亚音速螺旋流的时间周期解的存在性与稳定性，且无需对背景亚音速解施加小量限制。

Conclusion: 证明了在耗散/非耗散混合边界条件下，环形区域内非等熵欧拉系统存在稳定的时间周期解，为相关流体动力学问题提供了理论依据。

Abstract: We investigate subsonic time-periodic solutions to the radially symmetric non-isentropic Euler system with nonzero angular velocity in an annulus. Under the assumption that the boundary conditions are dissipative on the inner circle and non-dissipative on the outer circle, we establish the existence and stability of time-periodic solutions which are close to steady radially symmetric subsonic spiral flows. It is worth noting that there is no smallness restriction on the background subsonic solutions. The main difficulties arise from the derivative loss caused by the coupling with the radial entropy derivative and the additional zeroth-order terms induced by the nonzero angular velocity in the diagonalized system. One of the key ingredients of the analysis is to rewrite the radial derivative of the entropy as a derivative along the first or fourth characteristic direction. Another one is to control the accumulation of perturbations along characteristic curves by suitably restricting the width of the annulus.

</details>


### [29] [Short-time behavior and invariant surfaces for caloric functions with non-constant boundary values](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18784)
*Diego Berti,Rolando Magnanini,Michele Marini*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文研究了具有变系数非散度形式热方程的柯西-狄利克雷问题，推导了短时间渐近公式（推广了Varadhan公式），允许边界值变号或为零，并证明了椭圆对应公式、热含量及球面上平均值公式，进而应用于时间不变曲面的对称性与不存在性分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 针对非散度形式热方程在非齐次Dirichlet边界条件下的短时间渐近行为，经典Varadhan公式仅适用于齐次边界条件或特定情形，本文旨在将Varadhan公式推广到允许边界值变号或为零的更一般情形，并探索其在时间不变曲面问题中的应用。

Method: 结合Varadhan的原始思想与Evans-Ishii的粘性解理论，通过渐近分析方法推导热方程解的短时间渐近公式；同时利用椭圆方程对应的慢扩散行为得到椭圆版本公式；对经典Laplace算子，进一步推导热含量和球面上平均值公式，并利用这些公式分析时间不变曲面的对称性。

Result: 得到了非散度形式热方程在非齐次Dirichlet边界条件下的短时间渐近公式（推广的Varadhan公式）；证明了椭圆对应公式；对经典Laplace算子，推导了热含量和球面上平均值在接触点处涉及主曲率和边界值的渐近公式；给出了非负Dirichlet边界值情形下的两个对称性结果，以及边界值变号时的非存在性结果。

Conclusion: 成功将Varadhan公式推广到变系数非散度形式热方程的非齐次Dirichlet边界情形，建立了短时间渐近行为与边界值、几何量（主曲率）之间的联系，并揭示了时间不变曲面的对称性与边界值符号的依赖关系。

Abstract: We consider a Cauchy-Dirichlet problem for a heat equation with variable coefficients in non-divergence form. The initial values are assumed to be homogeneous, while the Dirichlet boundary values are non-constant. In this setting, we derive an asymptotic formula for the short-time behavior of the solution, which extends the celebrated Varadhan formula. We stress the fact that the boundary values are allowed to vanish or change sign. The formula is obtained by combining the original ideas of Varadhan with those of Evans and Ishii, pertaining to the theory of viscosity solutions, and some further remarks. In passing, we prove the elliptic counterpart of the formula. This concerns the slow-diffusion behavior of the solutions of the resolvent equation. Furthermore, for the case of the classical Laplace operator, we prove asymptotic formulas for the heat content and the mean value of the solution of the resolvent equation on spheres touching the boundary of the domain. These extend to the case of non-constant boundary values, certain formulas previously obtained by the second author and S. Sakaguchi. The formulas involve the principal curvatures at the touching point and the Dirichlet boundary values. We then use our formulas to describe time-invariant surfaces for the heat equation, in presence of non-constant Dirichlet boundary values. We give two symmetry results in case of non-negative Dirichlet boundary values and a non-existence result, when those values change sign.

</details>


### [30] [Incompressible Navier-Stokes limit of non-bilinear kinetic equations and application to the BGK, nonlinear Fokker-Planck and Boltzmann-Fermi-Dirac equations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18939)
*Pierre Gervais*

Main category: math.AP

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用加权Sobolev空间中的定量分析，结合抽象动理学方程的熵耗散结构和谱方法策略，建立从动理学方程到Navier-Stokes-Fourier系统的统一收敛框架，并处理初始层问题。

Result: 在加权Sobolev空间中获得了向Navier-Stokes-Fourier系统的定量收敛结果，成功描述了初始层结构，并将适用模型从双线性碰撞推广到Boltzmann-Fermi-Dirac方程、BGK方程和非线性Fokker-Planck方程等非双线性情形。

Conclusion: 本文建立了一个统一的抽象框架，能够处理更广泛类型的动理学方程（包括非双线性碰撞模型）向流体力学系统的定量收敛问题，弥补了此前理论在非双线性模型上的空白。

Abstract: We consider collisional kinetic equations whose collision operator is not necessarily bilinear and prove quantitative convergence to the Navier-Stokes-Fourier system in weighted Sobolev spaces, together with a description of the initial layers. The aim of this paper is to conciliate the conditional convergence result of Bardos-Golse-Levermore for abstract kinetic equations conserving macroscopic quantities and dissipating entropy with the spectral strategy initiated by Bardos-Ukai for the Boltzmann equation. This work extends the abstract approach of Gervais-Lods which was restricted to bilinear collisions (Boltzmann, Landau or quadratic approximation of other models) to non-bilinear models such as the Boltzmann-Fermi-Dirac equation, the BGK equation and the nonlinear Fokker-Planck equation.

</details>


### [31] [Serrin problems with vertical boundary behavior](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18952)
*Julián Pozuelo,Simone Verzellesi*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 研究了一类可能退化椭圆算子的Serrin型超定问题，在迫使梯度爆破的垂直边界条件下，确定了问题在球上存在解的精确范围，并证明了刚性：解域必为球体，解由显式径向分布唯一确定。

Method: 通过分析退化椭圆算子的性质，确定问题在球上存在解的精确参数范围，并利用极值原理、移动平面法等工具证明解域的球对称性。

Result: 确定了问题在球上存在解的精确参数范围，并在该范围内证明了刚性结果：解域必须为球体，且解由显式的径向剖面唯一确定。

Abstract: We study Serrin-type overdetermined problems for a class of possibly degenerate elliptic operators under a vertical boundary condition forcing gradient blow-up. We identify the precise regime in which the problem admits a solution on a ball. In this regime, we prove rigidity: every solution domain is a ball, and the solution is uniquely determined by an explicit radial profile.

### [32] [Spreading dynamics for diffusive competition systems in shifting environments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19028)
*Thomas Giletti,Jong-Shenq Guo*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文研究气候变化引起的环境变化中，两种群扩散竞争系统的传播动力学，特别关注强-弱竞争情形下各物种灭绝与持续的条件，发现气候变化速度、物种竞争强弱、迁移速度及初始分布等因素会导致截然不同的种群动态结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究气候变化对多物种竞争系统的影响，特别是理解环境变化速度与物种竞争能力、扩散能力之间的交互作用如何决定物种的存亡，揭示气候变化下种群动态的复杂性。

Method: 对两物种扩散竞争系统进行数学建模，考虑环境变化导致的栖息地移动，分析强-弱竞争情形下的渐近行为，通过参数分岔研究气候变化速度、物种竞争强度、扩散速度及初始分布对解行为的影响。

Result: 发现了反直觉的结果：弱但扩散快的竞争者可能存活，而强但扩散慢的竞争者反而灭绝；存在参数区域，结果不仅取决于气候变化速度，还取决于两个物种对气候变化的恢复能力，甚至初始种群分布。

Conclusion: 气候变化对多物种种群动态的影响极其复杂，仅仅考虑单一物种或单一因素无法准确预测物种存亡，需要综合考量竞争关系、扩散能力和环境变化速率等多重因素。

Abstract: We study the spreading dynamics for two-species diffusive competition systems in shifting environments caused by climate changes. Our main goal is to derive conditions for extinction and persistence of each species in the case of a strong-weak competition. Depending on the pace of the climate change, but also on whether the strong competitor is faster or slower, we will uncover dramatically different outcomes in the asymptotic behavior of solutions. For instance, it may be that a weak and fast competitor survives while a strong and slow one does not. Furthermore, we find some parameter regime where the outcome depends not only on the climate change speed, but also on both species' resilience to it, and even on the initial populations' distributions. Our results show how strikingly complex the effect of climate change may be on population dynamics as soon as several species are considered.

Abstract: The hydrostatic balance is a fundamental equilibrium state in stratified fluids and plays a central role in geophysical fluid dynamics. Understanding its stability under incomplete dissipation is a longstanding challenge, since anisotropic diffusion alone is generally insufficient to control the nonlinear evolution and no robust stabilizing mechanism is known for the corresponding anisotropically dissipative Navier--Stokes equations. In this paper, we investigate the two-dimensional Boussinesq equations on $\mathbb{R}^2$ with only horizontal dissipation near the hydrostatic equilibrium $(U,Θ)=(0,x_2)$. We show that the velocity--temperature coupling generates internal gravity waves whose dispersive decay, together with the horizontal dissipation, provides an effective stabilizing mechanism that compensates for the complete absence of vertical dissipation. This identifies a mechanism by which dispersive wave propagation restores stability in an incompletely dissipative fluid system. For sufficiently small initial perturbations in $H^k(\mathbb{R}^2)\cap W^{3,1}(\mathbb{R}^2)$ with $k\ge14$, we establish the global existence and uniqueness of classical solutions together with explicit anisotropic, componentwise large-time decay rates for the velocity and temperature, including faster decay of the vertical velocity.

### [35] [Resolution of the ENO-TV conjecture: a parity dichotomy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19283)
*Zhuoyun Li,Kailiang Wu*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文解决了双曲守恒律熵稳定近似紧致性理论中的ENO-TV猜想。证明了奇数次(k≥3)ENO重构满足该估计，而偶数次(k≥4)不成立，形成了奇偶二分法。通过离散Gagliardo-Nirenberg不等式证明奇数次情形的强制性，通过Euler多项式块构造偶数次情形的反例。同时给出了对所有k≥2的两个强制性估计，并分析了网格几何对结果的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决ENO-TV猜想，这是一个关于双曲守恒律熵稳定近似紧致性理论中的离散强制性（coercivity）问题。该猜想询问：对于k阶本质无振荡（ENO）重构，非负ENO源乘以振幅的(k-1)次幂是否能一致地控制(k+1)次绝对跳跃矩。

Method: 1) 通过局部化将猜想简化为与选择无关的有限差分泛函和离散插值问题；2) 对奇数次情形，利用分部求和揭示隐藏平方项，再应用离散Gagliardo-Nirenberg不等式证明强制性；3) 对偶数次情形，利用泛函多项式核中的Euler多项式块构造反例；4) 通过Cayley-Sylvester分解计算格点平移在多项式跳跃剖面上的齐次第一上同调空间的维数；5) 分析全局拟均匀网格和固定不规则网格上的表现。

Result: 1) 奇偶二分法：对于奇数次k≥3成立，偶数次k≥4不成立，结合已知的二阶情形完成分类；2) 偶数次反例在任意小扰动下依然成立（即使所有ENO比较都变为严格）；3) 对所有k≥2证明两个强制性估计；4) 四阶情形下，对于三次通量和全局严格凸熵，约化熵-通量不匹配的一个全七次分量在至多二次剖面上表示非零类，因此在零常数态处没有平移不变的有限模板C^7局部原像；5) 奇数次强制性在全局拟均匀网格上保持，但每个k≥2在固定不规则网格上失效（即使所有界面贡献非负），失效源于网格几何。

Conclusion: 完整解决了ENO-TV猜想，建立了奇偶二分法的严格分类。该结果揭示了ENO重构的深层结构性质，包括多项式核、上同调结构和网格几何对离散强制性的影响，为双曲守恒律的熵稳定数值方法提供了紧致性理论基础。

Abstract: We resolve the ENO--TV conjecture, a discrete coercivity problem in compactness theory for entropy-stable approximations of hyperbolic conservation laws. For order-$k$ essentially non-oscillatory (ENO) reconstruction from compactly supported cell averages, it asks whether the nonnegative ENO source times the $(k-1)$st power of the amplitude uniformly controls the $(k+1)$st absolute-jump moment. We prove a parity dichotomy: the estimate holds for odd $k\ge3$ and fails for even $k\ge4$; the known second-order case completes the classification. Localization gives a selection-independent finite-difference functional uniformly comparable to the source and reduces the conjecture to discrete interpolation. For odd orders, summation by parts reveals a hidden square; a discrete Gagliardo--Nirenberg inequality yields coercivity. For even orders, Euler-polynomial blocks from the functional's polynomial kernel yield counterexamples that persist under arbitrarily small perturbations making all affected ENO comparisons strict. We also prove two coercive estimates for every $k\ge2$: control of jumps larger than a fixed fraction of the amplitude and of local blocks modulo sampled polynomials of degree at most $k-2$. Via the Cayley--Sylvester decomposition, we compute the dimensions of homogeneous first-cohomology spaces for the lattice shift on polynomial jump profiles. At fourth order, for a cubic flux and a globally strictly convex entropy, a total-degree-seven component of a reduced entropy-flux mismatch represents a nonzero class on profiles of degree at most two and hence has no translation-invariant finite-stencil $C^7$ local primitive at the zero constant state. Odd-order coercivity persists on globally quasi-uniform meshes, whereas for each $k\ge2$ it fails on a fixed irregular mesh even though every interface contribution remains nonnegative. This failure is due to the mesh geometry.

</details>


### [36] [Classification of spherical metrics on tori with four singularities, I: half periods](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19073)
*Erjuan Fu,Chang-Shou Lin*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文研究环面 $E_τ$ 上在四个半周期点处具有 $4π$ 锥角的球面度量的分类问题，等价于求解带有 Dirac 源的曲率方程 $\Delta u + e^u = 4π\sum δ_{ω_k/2}$。通过构造多重 Green 函数 $G_2$，将解分为特殊解与非特殊解两类：特殊解为偶函数，其集合同构于 $SL(2,\mathbb{C})/SU(2)$；非特殊解存在当且仅当 $τ\in \mathcal{E}$，此时存在六个单参数族解。同时完全确定了 $G_2$ 的临界点及其退化准则。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 分类环面上在四个半周期点处具有 $4π$ 锥角的球面度量，这类问题具有重要的几何与物理意义，其核心是求解相应的曲率方程。

Method: 利用环面 Green 函数 $G(z;τ)$ 构造多重 Green 函数 $G_2(z_1,z_2;τ)$，并基于此将方程解的临界点分类为特殊与非特殊两类，进而分析解的结构与存在性。

Result: 任何特殊解为偶函数，且其集合同构于 $SL(2,\mathbb{C})/SU(2)$；非特殊解存在当且仅当 $τ\in\mathcal{E}$（临界点恰好5个的模参数），此时存在六个单参数族非特殊解。$\mathcal{E}$ 由可数多个开三角形区域组成。同时完全确定了 $G_2$ 的临界点及其退化准则。

Conclusion: 给出了环面上特定锥角球面度量的完整分类，建立了解结构与模参数 $τ$ 之间的精确对应关系，并提供了 $G_2$ 临界点理论的独立结果。

Abstract: Classifying the spherical metrics on a torus $E_τ$ with $4π$ conic angle at each half period point\, ${ω_k}/{2}, k=0,1,2,3$\, is equivalent to classify solutions of the following curvature equation \begin{align}\label{eq0731093154}
  Δu+e^u=4π\sum_{k=0}^3δ_{\frac{ω_k}{2}}\text{\ on\ }E_τ\end{align} where $τ\in \mathbb{H}:=\{z\in \mathbb{C}\mid \mathrm{Im} \, z>0\}$ and $δ_p$ is the Dirac measure at $p\in E_τ$.
  By constructing a multiple Green function $$G_2(z_1, z_2;τ):=G(z_1-z_2;τ)-\frac{1}{2}\sum_{j=0}^3\left(G(z_1-\frac{ω_j}{2};τ)+G(z_2-\frac{ω_j}{2};τ)\right), $$ in terms of the Green function $G(z;τ)$ on $E_τ$, we classify the solutions of (\ref{eq0731093154}) into two types: \emph{special} and \emph{non-special}. Furthermore, we obtain the following conclusion about the solutions of (\ref{eq0731093154}): \begin{enumerate} \item any special solution is an even function and the set of special solutions is isomorphic to $SL(2,\mathbb{C})/SU(2)$ for all $τ\in \mathbb{H}$. \item a non-special solution exists if and only if $τ\in \mathcal{E}$. Moreover, if $τ\in \mathcal{E}$, then there are six one-parameter families of nonspecial solutions. \end{enumerate} where $$\mathcal{E}:=\left\{τ\in \mathbb{H}\mid G(z;τ) \,\,\text{has exactly 5 critical points.}\right\}.$$ The set $\mathcal{E}$ is completely determined in \cite{CLW2018, Lin}, which is a union of countable many open triangular domains. As a byproduct, we completely determine and classify the critical points of $G_2$ and then obtain the degeneracy criterion of critical points for $G_2$, which may be of independent interest.

Abstract: We investigate time-periodic dynamics in a forager-exploiter system with a taxis cascade under both homogeneous and heterogeneous resource environments. The model describes the interactions among foragers, exploiters, and environmental resources, where foragers move toward higher resource densities while exploiters aggregate toward regions with higher forager densities. Our results show that different resource renewal mechanisms shape periodic dynamics in fundamentally different ways. Precisely, for time-periodic resource renewal rates, we establish the existence of positive time-periodic solutions for any positive renewal rate and further prove their global stability under suitable conditions on the parameters. In contrast, for homogeneous environments, only large resource renewal rates can destabilize the constant steady state through the Hopf bifurcation, thereby generating non-constant time-periodic solutions.

When resources are sufficiently abundant, spatial heterogeneity tends to suppress the emergence of temporal oscillations, whereas when resources are relatively scarce, it may instead promote oscillatory behaviors, and sufficiently concentrated local resource supplies can trigger local or even global temporal oscillations. These findings reveal a delicate interplay among resource renewal mechanisms, resource availability, and spatial heterogeneity in shaping dynamics behavior.

### [41] [Good access to the crack and integrability of the full gradient for Griffith almost-minimizers in the plane](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19229)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究的动机在于深入理解Griffith断裂准则下裂纹体的正则性性质，尤其是在二维情形下，对于几乎极小化问题，裂纹补集的结构以及位移场的正则性尚未得到充分刻画。

Method: 本文通过分析几乎极小化问题的几何和解析性质，利用John域覆盖理论以及Hölder型估计方法，结合变分法技巧，对裂纹补集进行精细的分解与估计，进而推导全梯度的可积性和迹的有限性。

Result: 得到了裂纹补集被有限个John域局部覆盖，位移在这些域上满足Hölder型估计；同时证明了全梯度的可积性和裂纹上迹的有限性；最终确立了二维Griffith几乎极小化问题局部属于SBV^2空间。

Conclusion: 该工作为二维Griffith能量几乎极小化问题提供了更加精细的正则性理论，为断裂力学中裂纹扩展和材料破坏的数学模型提供了坚实的分析基础。

Abstract: We show that, for almost-minimizers of the Griffith energy in the plane, the complement of the crack is locally covered by a finite number of John domains where the displacement satisfies Hölder-type estimates. As a consequence, we derive the integrability of the full gradient and the finiteness of the traces along the crack. In particular, we show that any Griffith almost-minimizer in dimension two locally belongs to the space SBV^2.

</details>


### [42] [Vortex-sheet desingularization for three-dimensional ideal fluids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19233)
*Alberto Enciso,Antonio J. Fernández,David Meyer*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文证明了一个关于3D不可压缩欧拉方程解析涡面的去奇异化定理：对任意足够小的厚度参数ε>0，在涡面附近的O(ε)宽度的管状邻域内构造出精确的欧拉涡量，其定义的时间区间不随ε→0而收缩，并且这些涡量在分布意义下收敛到指定的涡面。从而证明了解析3D涡面运动可以在ε独立有界的时间区间内被精确欧拉流逼近。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构造依赖于时间的近平行曲面叶状结构，并在这些曲面上定义无散的切向向量场，从而在涡面周围的管状邻域内构造出精确的欧拉涡量。核心是利用Birkhoff-Rott系统的解析解作为初始逼近，通过小参数ε控制厚度。

Result: 对任意足够小的ε>0，成功构造了定义在ε独立有界时间区间上的精确欧拉涡量，其涡量支撑在涡面周围O(ε)宽度的管状邻域内，并在分布意义下收敛到原始涡面。

Conclusion: 三维解析涡面运动可以被厚度任意薄的精确欧拉流所逼近，且逼近的时间区间下界独立于厚度参数，从而建立了理想涡面模型与真实流体运动之间的严格数学联系。

Abstract: We prove a desingularization theorem for analytic vortex sheets of the 3D incompressible Euler equations. Starting from an analytic solution of the corresponding Birkhoff-Rott system, we construct, for every sufficiently small thickness parameter $\varepsilon>0 $, an exact Euler vorticity supported on a tubular neighborhood of width $ O(\varepsilon) $ around the sheet, and defined on a time interval that does not shrink to 0 as $\varepsilon \to 0$. We show that, as $\varepsilon \to 0$, these vorticities converge, in the sense of distributions, to the prescribed vortex sheet. In particular, we conclude that analytic 3D vortex sheet motions arise as limits of exact Euler flows with lifespan bounded from below independently of $ \varepsilon $. The proof hinges on the study of vorticities defined in terms of a time-dependent foliation by almost parallel surfaces and of divergence-free vector fields tangent to these surfaces.

### [44] [From zero solutions with partially bounded supports to solvability and Runge approximation for partial differential equations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19272)
*Tomasz Ciás,Thomas Kalmes*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文针对一大类常系数偏微分算子，建立了具有部分有界支撑的光滑零解的存在性，并由此推导出关于可解性和逼近的几何刻画，推广了Hörmander的P-凸性理论，同时发展了Runge型逼近的通用框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 齐次偏微分方程具有指定支撑性质的非平凡解的存在性是线性偏微分算子理论的基础问题。本文旨在建立更广泛的常系数偏微分算子的光滑零解的存在性，并由此导出可解性和逼近问题的几何刻画。

Method: 通过建立具有部分有界支撑的光滑零解的存在性定理，利用几何分析的方法刻画P-凸性；运用Malgrange定理将P-凸性与算子在全纯函数空间及局部有限阶分布子空间上的满射性相联系；发展Runge型逼近的统一框架，并应用于方型常系数偏微分方程组。

Result: 获得了非椭圆算子的支撑P-凸性的几何刻画；证明每个满射的半椭圆算子的核满足条件(Ω)；给出了光滑函数、分布和光滑Whitney jets的Runge对的几何刻画；恢复了Beltrami场和三维非定常Stokes系统的已知Runge逼近结果，并补充了光滑Whitney jets空间的逼近定理。

Conclusion: 本文为一大类常系数偏微分算子建立了支撑性质、可解性和Runge逼近的完整几何理论，推广了Hörmander的经典工作，并为带Hölder连续边界条件的适定域上的边界逼近提供了新方法。

Abstract: The existence of non-trivial solutions of homogeneous partial differential equations with prescribed support properties plays a fundamental role in the theory of linear partial differential operators. In this article, we establish the existence of smooth zero solutions with partially bounded supports for a broad class of constant coefficient partial differential operators.
  As applications, we obtain new geometric results concerning solvability and approximation for partial differential equations. In particular, we derive geometric characterizations of $P$-convexity for supports for a large class of non-elliptic operators, thereby extending classical geometric ideas of Hörmander. By a theorem of Malgrange, $P$-convexity for supports is equivalent to the surjectivity of the differential operator on spaces of smooth functions and, more generally, on local subspaces of distributions of finite order. As a further consequence, we prove that the kernel of every surjective semi-elliptic operator satisfies condition ($Ω$) implying parameter dependence results.
  We also investigate Runge-type approximation phenomena. We obtain geometric characterizations of Runge pairs for smooth functions, distributions, and spaces of smooth Whitney jets. Finally, we develop a general framework for Runge approximation for square systems of constant coefficient partial differential equations. As applications, we recover by alternative methods known Runge approximation results for Beltrami fields and for the three-dimensional unsteady Stokes system, and we complement them by corresponding approximation theorems in spaces of smooth Whitney jets. In particular, this yields approximation up to the boundary for solutions on suitable domains with Hölder continuous boundary.
