### [207] [Off-Context GRPO: Learning to Reason on Hard Problems using Privileged Information](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19313)
*Priyank Agrawal,Ankur Samanta,Shervin Ghasemlou,Jalaj Bhandari,Kavosh Asadi,Daniel Jiang,Aditya Modi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出Off-Context GRPO (OC-GRPO)，通过引入特权引导（如解答前缀）生成具有非零奖励的rollout，并利用重要性校正目标函数避免引导训练与原始无引导目标之间的偏差，在数学推理基准上平均提升3.9%的绝对性能（13.8%的相对提升），且额外成本可忽略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准RLVR方法在困难问题上失效：当模型无法生成任何正确解时，奖励信号为零，无法提供学习信号。为克服这一"学习悬崖"，需要提供特权引导（如解答前缀）来引导模型走向正确答案并获得非零奖励。

Method: 提出OC-GRPO，是GRPO的轻量变体。核心创新包括：(1) 使用包含特权引导（解答前缀）的训练提示生成rollout，称为"off-context" rollout；(2) 应用重要性校正目标函数，将更新方向校正回原始无引导目标，避免引导训练与原始目标之间的不匹配导致训练不稳定。

Result: 在标准数学推理基准上，OC-GRPO相比vanilla GRPO平均实现3.9%的绝对性能提升（13.8%的相对提升），且额外计算成本可忽略不计。

Conclusion: 通过off-context rollout和重要性校正，OC-GRPO有效解决了RLVR在困难问题上的学习信号缺失问题，同时避免了引导训练的目标偏移，实现了高效且稳定的推理能力提升。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) improves reasoning in large language models. Yet, typical RLVR approaches fail on difficult problems: when a model cannot generate any correct solutions, it receives \textit{zero} learning signal. Providing privileged guidance during training, such as solution prefixes, can help overcome this learning cliff by steering the model towards {correct solutions with non-zero reward}. {We call these rollouts \textit{off-context}: they are generated from a training prompt that contains privileged guidance, while the target objective is defined by the original prompt without that guidance.} {We introduce} Off-Context GRPO (OC-GRPO), a minimally modified variant of GRPO that uses guided rollouts but applies an importance-corrected objective to steer the update back toward the original unguided objective, avoiding the mismatch that destabilizes uncorrected guided training. Empirically, our algorithm achieves a 3.9\% absolute improvement (13.8\% relative gain) over vanilla GRPO on average across standard mathematical reasoning benchmarks with negligible additional cost.

</details>


### [208] [CircuitKIT : Circuit Discovery, Evaluation, and Application Toolkit for Mechanistic Interpretability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19317)
*Pratinav Seth,Hem Gosalia,Aditya Kasliwal,Vinay Kumar Sankarapu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: CircuitKIT是一个开源库，通过类型化、可序列化的表示连接电路分析工作流，集成了发现算法、声明式接口、诊断工具和下游应用模块，旨在解决电路分析方法碎片化、难以比较和复用的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前电路分析需要拼接不同的实现来完成发现、评估和干预，方法碎片化严重，难以比较，且仅限于规范任务，缺乏统一的基础设施。

Method: 提出CircuitKIT库，核心是类型化可序列化表示，整合了多种发现算法、声明式接口（将结构化数据映射为发现任务）、互补诊断工具以及下游应用模块（剪枝、编辑、引导、选择性微调）。

Result: 构建了一个统一的电路分析工作流基础设施，支持从发现到干预的完整流程，并开源了代码、示例、笔记本和文档。

Conclusion: CircuitKIT通过统一的表示和模块化设计，降低了电路分析的门槛，促进了方法的比较和复现，拓展了电路分析在下游任务中的应用。

Abstract: Circuit analysis can support not only model explanation but also downstream interventions such as pruning, editing, steering, and selective fine-tuning. However, conducting such analyses currently requires stitching together separate implementations for discovery, evaluation, and intervention, as well as hand-authoring the contrastive prompts required by many discovery methods. This fragmentation makes methods difficult to compare and limits their application beyond canonical tasks. We introduce CircuitKIT, a source-available library that connects the circuit-analysis workflow through a typed, serializable representation. CircuitKIT provides a suite of discovery algorithms, declarative interfaces for mapping structured data into discovery tasks, complementary circuit diagnostics, and downstream application modules. Together, these components provide common infrastructure for conducting and comparing circuit analyses. The library, examples, notebooks, and documentation are released at https://github.com/Lexsi-Labs/CircuitKIT .

### [209] [ISO: An RLVR-Native Optimization Stack](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19331)
*Hanqing Zhu,Wenyan Cong,Zhizhou Sha,Sagnik Mukherjee,Xinyuan Song,David González-Martínez,Xiaoxia Wu,Yuandong Tian,Shiwei Liu,David Z. Pan,Zhangyang "Atlas" Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出等谱优化（ISO）框架，揭示强化学习与可验证奖励（RLVR）训练中的“谱继承”现象：模型保留基模型的权重谱（奇异值），仅通过学习输入/输出奇异帧的变化来获得新行为。ISO包含离线（ISO-Merger）和在线（ISO-Optimizer）两种实例，在推理和编码任务上显著提升效率，例如ISO-AdamW用100步达到AdamW 270步的精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: RLVR在提升语言模型推理能力方面进展迅速，但其将奖励反馈转化为权重空间更新的优化层机制尚不清晰，存在“缺失的优化层”问题。

Method: 通过模型权重的奇异结构分析，识别出“谱继承”现象，并据此提出等谱优化（ISO）框架：离线版ISO-Merger通过合并共享基模型专家的帧变化实现无数据合并；在线版ISO-Optimizer固定基模型谱，仅优化帧变量，可集成AdamW、Muon等基优化器。

Result: 在1.5B到8B参数的推理和编码任务上，ISO-Merger在无数据合并方法中取得最佳聚合性能；ISO-Optimizer显著减少训练步数，Qwen3-8B-Base上ISO-AdamW用100步达到AdamW 270步的0.495精度，210步进一步提升至0.509。

Conclusion: ISO为RLVR提供了具体的优化层设计方案：后训练应围绕奖励驱动适应的结构进行设计，即继承谱、优化帧，而非全盘继承预训练优化方式。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) is rapidly advancing the reasoning capabilities of language models, yet the optimization layer that converts reward feedback into weight-space updates remains poorly understood. Building on our prior analysis (Zhu et al., 2025), we study this missing layer through the singular structure of model weights and identify spectral inheritance: RLVR can reuse the base model's weight spectra while acquiring new behavior through changes in the associated input and output singular frames.
  We operationalize spectral inheritance as Isospectral Optimization (ISO), an RLVR-native, fixed-spectrum optimization framework with complementary offline and online instantiations. Offline, ISO-Merger combines the frame changes of shared-base specialists into a single fixed-spectrum model, requiring no post-merge data, rollouts, gradient updates, or on-policy distillation (OPD). It recovers complementary specialist capabilities and achieves the strongest aggregate performance among the compared data-free merging methods. Online, ISO-Optimizer applies a chosen base optimizer, including AdamW and Muon, to the frame variables while keeping the base spectra fixed. Across reasoning and coding tasks ranging from 1.5B to 8B parameters, ISO-Optimizer improves accuracy in the reported runs and reaches matched scores with substantially fewer training steps. On Qwen3-8B-Base, AdamW reaches an aggregate accuracy of 0.495 after 270 training steps. ISO-AdamW reaches the same accuracy after only 100 training steps and improves further to 0.509 after 210 training steps. Together, ISO offers a concrete answer to RLVR's missing optimization layer: rather than inheriting pre-training optimization wholesale, design post-training around the structure of reward-driven adaptation: inherit the spectrum, optimize the frames.

</details>


### [210] [ROMS-IMLE: A Minimalist Approach to Competitive Single-Step Generative Modelling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19332)
*Chirag Vashist,Ke Li*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文质疑了扩散/流匹配模型中"逐步去噪"的必要性，采用极简主义方法，仅使用IMLE训练目标和中等规模卷积网络，构建了一个单步生成模型，在ImageNet 256上达到FID 2.56，同时具有良好的精度和召回率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 质疑当前生成模型领域中"通过许多小变换逐步将噪声分布转化为数据分布"这一普遍信念的必要性，探索是否能以更简化的方式设计出具有竞争力的生成模型。

Method: 采用极简主义方法：训练目标选择IMLE（隐式最大似然估计），避免变分推断、对抗训练和数值积分等复杂方案；模型选择中等规模卷积网络而非Transformer；仅添加真正必要的元素，刻意不包含迭代去噪过程。

Result: 构建的单步生成模型在ImageNet 256上实现了2.56的FID分数，同时保持了良好的精度和召回率，且参数效率高、生成速度快。

Conclusion: 迭代去噪并非高性能生成模型的必要组件，通过精心选择的训练目标和模型架构，单步生成即可达到竞争性表现，挑战了当前扩散/流匹配模型的核心理念。

Abstract: Generative models have undergone many generations of evolution, from VAEs/GANs to diffusion/flow matching. Along the way, the underlying techniques have become more complicated and various beliefs about what drives strong empirical performance have taken hold. Due to the success of diffusion models and flow matching, one of the more common beliefs is the importance of transforming the noise distribution to the data distribution gradually through many small transformations. We ask whether this is truly necessary, and take a minimalist approach to designing a competitive generative model. We start with the bare-bones essentials, namely just a training objective and a model. We purposefully make both simple. For the training objective, we choose Implicit Maximum Likelihood Estimation (IMLE), and eschew more complicated alternatives such as variational inference, adversarial training and numerical integration. For the model, we eschew transformers and instead choose a moderately sized convolutional network. Then we judiciously added elements that are truly essential, which surprisingly do not include iterative denoising. The result is a single-step parameter-efficient generative model that produces high quality samples at fast speed: it achieves an FID of 2.56 on ImageNet 256 and simultaneously attains good precision and recall.

</details>
